PMP Exam 4
Question 1 of 200
Question ID: 612094
Project execution has just begun. As the project manager, you want to ensure the work is being
performed according to the required quality standards.
What is your best course of action?
- **A Implement the quality management plan using the appropriate tools and techniques**
- **B Verify that the project deliverables conform to the standards established in the quality**
management plan
- **C Develop the quality management plan and define the quality standards for the project and**
its products
- **D Obtain feedback from relevant stakeholders to evaluate their satisfaction**
Question answered correctly

**Hint:**

You are in the Manage Quality process.
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The question states your project is in execution, and the scenario implies you want to carry out
the Manage Quality process. During the Manage Quality process, quality activities are performed
according to the quality management plan which was developed to incorporate the required
quality standards. Therefore, to ensure the work is being performed according to the required
quality standards, you need to implement the quality management plan using the tools and
techniques specified in the plan. Task 3 of Domain III in the Project Management Professional
(PMP)® Examination Content Outline reads, "Implement the quality management plan using the
appropriate tools and techniques in order to ensure that work is performed in accordance with
required quality standards."

**Details for Each Option:**


---

- **A Implement the quality management plan using the appropriate tools and techniques**
Correct. During Manage Quality, which according to the scenario is the process you are
going to carry out, quality activities are performed according to the quality management
plan which was developed to incorporate the required quality standards. To ensure the
work is being performed according to the required quality standards, you need to
implement the quality management plan using the tools and techniques outlined in the plan.
- **B Verify that the project deliverables conform to the standards established in the quality**
management plan
Incorrect. Verifying the project deliverables is performed in the Control Quality process to
determine the correctness of the deliverables. According to the scenario, you want to
ensure the work is being performed according to the required quality standards rather than
determine the correctness of the deliverables.
- **C Develop the quality management plan and define the quality standards for the project and**
its products
Incorrect. Developing the quality management plan is the main activity of the Plan Quality
Management process which is part of the Planning Process Group. The scenario suggests
the project is execution; therefore, the quality management plan has already been
developed.
- **D Obtain feedback from relevant stakeholders to evaluate their satisfaction**
Incorrect. Obtaining feedback from stakeholders to evaluate their satisfaction is typically
performed as part of the Close Project or Phase process after the customer has accepted
the completed deliverable. In the scenario, the project is in execution and concerned with
the quality of the work being performed. Therefore, obtaining feedback from stakeholders
is not what you should do.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 288; see also Project Management Professional
(PMP)® Examination Content Outline, Project Management Institute Inc., June 2015, Domain
III, Task 3
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results
Next

PMP Exam 4
Question 2 of 200
Question ID: 610058
- **A project is divided into four sequential phases. The second phase of the project has just been**
completed, and the third phase is about to begin.
What should the project manager do first?
- **A Begin the process of directing and managing the project work**
- **B Perform the process of identifying the project stakeholders**
- **C Start the process of monitoring and controlling the project work**
- **D Begin the process of developing the project management plan**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

- **A new phase should begin with the Initiating Process Group.**
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The process of identifying project stakeholders occurs for the first time in a project either before
or at the same time the project charter is developed and approved. It is repeated as necessary but
should be performed at the start of each phase and when a significant change in the project or
organization occurs. Each time the identification process is repeated, the project management
plan components and project documents should be consulted to identify relevant project
stakeholders.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Begin the process of directing and managing the project work**
Incorrect. A project or a new phase of an existing project is started with the Initiating
Process Group. The Direct and Manage Project Work process is part of the Executing

---

Process Group. Therefore, this answer choice can be eliminated.
- **B Perform the process of identifying the project stakeholders**
Correct. The Initiating Process Group is made up of two project management processes,
Develop Project Charter and Identify Stakeholders. The Initiating Process Group is
performed to define a new project or a new phase of an existing project by obtaining
authorization to start the project or phase. Of the available options, only the Identify
Stakeholders process is part of the Initiating Process Group and, therefore, is the best
answer to the question asked.
- **C Start the process of monitoring and controlling the project work**
Incorrect. The Monitor and Control Project Work process is part of the Monitoring and
Controlling Process Group. The phase must be initiated, planned, and execution must be
underway before there can be any project work to monitor and control.
- **D Begin the process of developing the project management plan**
Incorrect. The Develop Project Management Plan process is part of the Planning Process
Group. A phase is started with the Initiating Process Group and not the Planning Process
Group, making this an incorrect answer.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 508
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 4
Question 3 of 200
Question ID: 612632
- **A project manager contracted a vendor to develop the software for a new billing system. Shortly**
after the deliverables were formally accepted, the system crashed leading to downtime and a
substantial financial loss. An internal investigation concluded that a computer virus had been
residing in the new software due to the vendor's negligence.
After the claim with the vendor is settled, what is the best way to prevent this issue from
recurring?
- **A Record the final resolution of the problem in the issue log**
- **B Capture the situation and its resolution in the lessons learned register**
- **C Update the risk register with the implementation of the risk response**
- **D Conduct future software development projects with only internal resources**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which response represents an action which supports continuous improvement?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The lessons learned register is a project document used to record knowledge gained during a
project so that it can be used to improve the performance of the current project. At the end of the
project, the information contained in the lessons learned register is then transferred to an
organizational process asset called the lessons learned repository for use in future projects. Any
information regarding claims and how they were resolved should be documented in the lessons
learned register to avoid recurrences in the future. Note, the question does not explicitly mention
future projects. It reads, "What is the best way to prevent this issue from recurring?" Even
though future projects are not mentioned, it can be implied. Additionally, the question suggests
the current project is over. Therefore, preventing this issue from recurring infers recurring in
future projects. Therefore, of the available choices, capturing the knowledge gained in the
lessons learned register is the best way to prevent the problem from recurring.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Record the final resolution of the problem in the issue log**
Incorrect. It is not known from the question whether the problem was captured in the issue
log. Assuming it was, then the final resolution should be recorded as a project document
update. However, the issue log will not make the information available for use in future
projects, so this action is not the best way to prevent a recurrence of the issue.
- **B Capture the situation and its resolution in the lessons learned register**
Correct. Information regarding any claims and how they were resolved should be
documented in the lessons learned register to avoid recurrences in the future.
- **C Update the risk register with the implementation of the risk response**
Incorrect. The question does not specify if the risk of a computer virus was identified
earlier in the project. If this risk was captured in the risk register, then it may be updated
with status changes and finally closed out. However, the risk register from the current
project does not serve as an input for future projects, and the knowledge gained would be
lost.
- **D Conduct future software development projects with only internal resources**
Incorrect. Using only internal resources would allow more control over the project.
However, the performing organization may not have internal resources with the necessary
skillset. Additionally, a computer virus could still be an issue even with using internal
resources. Therefore, just using in-house developers is not likely to prevent the problem
from occurring in the future.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 500
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results
Prev Next

PMP Exam 4
Question 4 of 200
Question ID: 612627
- **A project manager is in the process of developing the risk management plan. The project**
manager has just pulled a blank template of a risk breakdown structure (RBS) from the
organizational process assets.
What should the project manager do next?
- **A Determine the risk categories**
- **B Develop a comprehensive list of project risks**
- **C Create the risk register**
- **D Develop responses to individual project risks**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which answer choice describes an activity associated with an element of the risk management
plan?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The question implies that the Plan Risk Management process is underway with the development
of the risk management plan. One of the elements of the risk management plan is risk categories.
Risk categories provide a means for grouping individual project risks. A common way to
structure risk categories is with a risk breakdown structure (RBS), which is a hierarchical
representation of potential sources of risk. An RBS helps the project team consider the full range
of sources from which individual project risks may arise. This approach may help during the
Identify Risks process to identify individual project risks as well as sources of overall project
risks. The incorrect answer choices represent actions associated with Project Risk Management
processes other than Plan Risk Management. Therefore, after obtaining a blank template of an
RBS, the next logical step is to determine the risk categories for inclusion in the RBS.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Determine the risk categories**
Correct. One of the elements of the risk management plan is risk categories. Risk
categories provide a means for grouping individual project risks. A common way to
structure risk categories is with a risk breakdown structure (RBS).
- **B Develop a comprehensive list of project risks**
Incorrect. The development of the risk management plan indicates that the Plan Risk
Management process is underway. A comprehensive list of project risks is developed
during the Identify Risks process which follows the Plan Risk Management process.
- **C Create the risk register**
Incorrect. The question implies that the Plan Risk Management process is being performed.
The risk register is created as an output of the Identify Risks process, rather than the Plan
Risk Management process.
- **D Develop responses to individual project risks**
Incorrect. The development of responses to individual project risks is part of the Plan Risk
Responses process which comes later in project risk planning. The scenario describes the
development of the risk management plan which precedes risk identification and the
development of the responses to those risks.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 405
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 4
Question 5 of 200
Question ID: 626016
- **A project manager has encountered a new issue during project execution and wants to document**
this issue in the issue log.
What should the project manager do first?
- **A Add the issue to the issue log**
- **B Submit a change request to update the issue log**
- **C Analyze the impact of the issue and submit a change request to update the issue log**
- **D Consult the issue management plan on how to manage new issues on the project**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The issue log is not a part of the project management plan.
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The issue log is a project document used by the project teams to document issues they encounter
on the project. Unlike the project management plan, which is a controlled document, the issue
log is a project document and not a part of the project management plan. To be updated, the issue
log does not require a change request. When a new issue arises on the project, the project
manager should first add the issue to the issue log, assign an owner and a target resolution date.
The issue log should then be reviewed regularly to ensure the issues are addressed. No change
request is needed when an uncontrolled document has to be updated. However, if the resolution
of the issue will require the project team to take actions that will eventually affect any of the
components of the project management plan, which is a controlled document, then a change
request should be submitted and processed accordingly.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

- **A Add the issue to the issue log**
Correct. When a new issue arises throughout the course of a project, the issue should be
added to the issue log.
- **B Submit a change request to update the issue log**
Incorrect. The issue log is not a controlled document and does not require a change
request to be updated.
- **C Analyze the impact of the issue and submit a change request to update the issue log**
Incorrect. While an impact of the issue on the project can and should be analyzed, and any
further actions taken, entering the issue into the issue log should be the first step. Again,
the issue log is not a controlled document and does not require a change request to be
updated.
- **D Consult the issue management plan on how to manage new issues on the project**
Incorrect. 'Issue management plan' is a fake term made up for this question.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 96
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 4
Question 6 of 200
Question ID: 612439
- **A project manager has been authorized to apply organizational resources to a new project.**
What should the project manager do next?
- **A Develop the summary milestone schedule**
- **B Create the assumption log**
- **C Develop the project business documents**
- **D Finalize the project charter**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Try to eliminate the activities, which have already been done.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The question states that the project manager has been authorized to apply organizational
resources to the project, implying the project charter has been approved as part of the Develop
Project Charter process. However, it does not necessarily mean that the process itself has been
completed. At that point, the project business documents such as the benefits management plan
and the business case would have been used as inputs to the Develop Project Charter process, the
project charter would be finalized, and the summary milestone schedule would exist as part of
the project charter. By process of elimination, the project manager should next create the
assumption log, which is, in addition to the project charter, an output of the Develop Project
Charter process.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Develop the summary milestone schedule**

---

Incorrect. By saying that the project manager has been authorized to apply organizational
resources to a new project, the question suggests that the project charter has been created
and approved. The summary milestone schedule is part of the project charter and,
therefore, should have already been developed.
- **B Create the assumption log**
Correct. It can be implied from the scenario, that the project is in the Develop Project
Charter process. In addition to the project charter, the assumption log is an output of this
process.
- **C Develop the project business documents**
Incorrect. The project business documents include the business case and benefits
management plan. These documents are created during pre-project work and serve as
inputs into the Develop Project Charter process inferred by the scenario. Since the
question implies that the project charter has already been approved, the business
documents would have been developed previously.
- **D Finalize the project charter**
Incorrect. The project charter provides the project manager with the authority to apply
organizational resources to project activities. According to the scenario, the project
manager has been authorized to apply organizational resources to a new project.
Therefore, it can be assumed the project charter has already been finalized.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 81
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 4
Question 7 of 200
Question ID: 612588
You are in the planning stage of a large project, which will require contracts with various
vendors and suppliers to produce the project's deliverables. With the procurement management
plan and make-or-buy analysis complete, you are about to begin the development of a document
that will outline the procurement strategy for the project.
Which of the following are you least likely to include in this document?
- **A Procurement delivery methods**
- **B Type of agreements**
- **C Responsibilities of stakeholders**
- **D Procurement phases**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The question is asking for the element that is 'least' likely to be included in the procurement
strategy. One of the answer choices should be included in the procurement management plan
rather than the procurement strategy.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The procurement strategy is determined as part of the Plan Procurement Management process.
The procurement strategy, an output from this process, is comprised of three elements which
include procurement delivery methods, type of agreements, and procurement phases. The
question is asking for the element which is 'least' likely to be included in the procurement
strategy. The responsibilities of stakeholders, as it pertains to procurements, is an element of the
procurement management plan rather than the procurement strategy. Therefore, of the available
options, the responsibilities of stakeholders is the best answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

- **A Procurement delivery methods**
Incorrect. This answer choice represents one of the three elements typically included in the
procurement strategy.
- **B Type of agreements**
Incorrect. The type of agreements is one of the three components that are typically included
in the procurement strategy.
- **C Responsibilities of stakeholders**
Correct. The responsibilities of stakeholders, as it pertains to procurements, is an element
of the procurement management plan rather than the procurement strategy.
- **D Procurement phases**
Incorrect. Procurement phases are generally included in the procurement strategy.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 476, 481

PMP Exam 4
Question 8 of 200
Question ID: 613738
You and your team are meeting to evaluate vendor proposals. One of the team members
previously worked with Company A and praised their professionalism and quality. Another team
member prefers Company B. Several other team members join the conversation by adding their
opinions.
What should you remind the team members to focus on to select a seller?
- **A Procurement statement of work (SOW)**
- **B Bid documents**
- **C Source selection criteria**
- **D Procurement management plan**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which procurement document is used in the evaluation of vendor proposals?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

Source selection criteria are a set of measurable attributes desired by the buyer which a seller is
required to meet or exceed to be selected for a contract. By focusing on source selection criteria,
a proposal can be evaluated quantitatively, thereby removing any personal biases.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Procurement statement of work (SOW)**
Incorrect. The procurement SOW provides sellers with a clearly stated set of goals,
requirements, and outcomes from which they can produce a proposal for the work they will
provide. In this scenario, the sellers' proposals have already been received. Therefore, this

---

is not a correct answer.
- **B Bid documents**
Incorrect. Bid documents are used to solicit proposals from prospective sellers. In this
scenario, the vendors' proposals have already been received. Therefore, this is not the
correct answer.
- **C Source selection criteria**
Correct. Source selection criteria are measurable and provide a quantitative basis for
evaluation of proposals thereby minimizing personal biases. The source selection criteria
are the best thing for your project team to focus on when choosing the vendor.
- **D Procurement management plan**
Incorrect. The procurement management plan details the activities to be undertaken during
the procurement process. Source selection criteria are part of the procurement documents,
not part of the procurement management plan. Therefore, this is not a correct answer.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 485, 478, 723
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 4
Question 9 of 200
Question ID: 613846
- **A project manager provides overall direction, training, and support to her cross-functional team,**
but entrusts the team to manage and track their own work assignments and make decisions as a
group. The project manager participates in regular team meetings to monitor the team's progress
and provide support, but generally stays out of discussions about workload or team decision
making.
What is the project manager employing to manage the team?
- **A Emotional intelligence**
- **B Self-organizing teams**
- **C Team building**
- **D Motivation**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

This methodology is commonly associated with agile project management frameworks.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

This is an example of a self-organizing team, where the project manager provides overall
direction and support while entrusting team members to make their own decisions and manage
the work. The other answer choices may be part of the project manager's management approach,
but self-organizing teams is the better answer choice.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Emotional intelligence**
Incorrect. Although the project manager may be using emotional intelligence to a certain

---

degree, that is not the primary technique or methodology she is applying to manage the
team.
- **B Self-organizing teams**
Correct. Self-organizing teams are often used for projects using agile approaches. In this
scenario, the project manager and the team have roles that are typical of a self-organizing
team. The project manager provides overall direction and support while entrusting the
team to manage their own work to get the job done.
- **C Team building**
Incorrect. Team building is conducting activities that enhance the team’s social relations
and build a collaborative and cooperative working environment. Although the project
manager is cultivating an environment that supports team building, this scenario is best
described as an example of a self-organizing team.
- **D Motivation**
Incorrect. Motivation is providing a reason for someone to act. Teams are motivated by
empowering them to participate in decision making and encouraging them to work
independently. Although this is an attractive answer choice because the project manager is
motivating the team to work independently and make their own decisions, the method he is
using to empower and motivate them is a self-organizing team approach.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 310, 341
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 4
Question 10 of 200
Question ID: 613684
You are managing a new needs assessment project. While you are analyzing the monthly
progress data your team has submitted, you notice that one of your project team members has
spent half as much time working on a project activity than you had planned.
What should you do?
- **A Reward the team member for finishing the activity ahead of schedule**
- **B Investigate further to determine if there is a problem**
- **C Issue a corrective action as you obviously overestimated the activity duration**
- **D Do nothing now and wait for the next month's progress data.**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The Monitor and Control Project Work process balances the demands of the all the knowledge
areas to control the project.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The Monitor and Control Project Work process is part of Integration Management. The project
manager must balance the demands of all the knowledge areas to control the project. You can't
get a good understanding of how the project is performing against the project plan by only
monitoring one aspect of the project, for example, one employee's activity report. Therefore,
further investigation needs to be completed before acting on data from one process.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Reward the team member for finishing the activity ahead of schedule**
Incorrect. You certainly want to reward employees for good work, but at this point, you

---

don't know if the activity was completed correctly or if the team member completed other
activities on time. A further investigation would be warranted.
- **B Investigate further to determine if there is a problem**
Correct. You can't get a good understanding of how the project is performing against the
project plan by only monitoring one aspect of the project. You should review both the
quality of the deliverables produced by the team member during the activity and whether
she met other planned milestones. Once you have investigated further, you will know if
there is a discrepancy between your planned and actual estimates.
- **C Issue a corrective action as you obviously overestimated the activity duration**
Incorrect. Just because the team member worked half the hours, you had planned for her to
work on an activity doesn't mean you estimated incorrectly. Perhaps there are other
reasons for the discrepancy. Once you have investigated further, you will know if there is a
discrepancy between your planned and actual estimates. Based on the result of your
investigation, you can issue a corrective action, if necessary.
- **D Do nothing now and wait for the next month's progress data.**
Incorrect. A project manager should be proactive. Waiting a month for new progress data
could allow a problem to worsen, if there is a problem, making this an incorrect choice.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 105-108
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results
Prev Next

PMP Exam 4
Question 11 of 200
Question ID: 612549
- **A project has been in execution for several months, and project communications have been sent**
out regularly. During a meeting with the customer, some of the stakeholders indicate they have
not received the most recent performance report, which is supposed to be sent out every two
weeks.
What should the project manager do first?
- **A Document the issue in the issue log**
- **B Update the lessons learned register**
- **C Review the communications management plan**
- **D Update the change log**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

How can a project manager ensure that a problem encountered on a project will be investigated
and resolved?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

An issue is a current condition or situation that may have an impact on the project objectives. A
project performance report that has not been received by some of the project stakeholders as
scheduled is an issue and should be documented in the issue log. The issue log is a project
document where all problems encountered during a project are recorded and tracked. The
scenario suggests the project is in the Manage Communications process. Updates to the issue log
are among the outputs of the Manage Communications process. By adding the issue to the issue
log, the project manager can effectively manage the issue so that it can be documented, tracked,
and eventually resolved. All the other answer choices may be suitable responses 'after' the issue
is recorded in the issue log, but the first thing the project manager should do is update the issue
log.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Document the issue in the issue log**
Correct. The issue log is a project document where all issues encountered during a project
are recorded and tracked. Having just become aware of the problem with the receipt of the
most recent performance reports, the project manager would first want to update the issue
log with the information so that the matter can be documented, tracked, and eventually
resolved.
- **B Update the lessons learned register**
Incorrect. The lessons learned register is updated with information on challenges
encountered and how they could have been avoided as well as approaches that worked
well. In the scenario described, the project manager has just been made aware that some of
the stakeholders did not receive the performance reports. There has not been any
investigation into why the reports were not received. Therefore, updating the lessons
learned register is premature.
- **C Review the communications management plan**
Incorrect. The communications management plan describes how project communications
will be handled as well as provides information on stakeholder communication
requirements including details on who is to receive which type of information. While the
project manager would want to review the plan to understand the stakeholders'
requirements, he would first want to ensure the situation is recorded and tracked by adding
the lack of performance reports to the issue log.
- **D Update the change log**
Incorrect. The change log is used to document information on changes that occur during a
project. The change log would have to be updated if a change is requested. However, based
on the scenario provided, the project manager has just discovered that some stakeholders
have not received the performance reports. Therefore, he does not have enough
information to determine what change, if at all, is required at this point.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 387, 96
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results
Prev Next

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 12 of 200
Question ID: 613706
You are managing the development of a new user interface. You have produced the first interim
deliverable for the project, which is currently being evaluated by the quality control department.
Last weekend, at the company barbecue, you spoke with several business development
executives and asked them what they thought about the interim deliverable. They shared how
they were satisfied with the deliverable and were pleased with the project's progress.
What best describes what you have done?
- **A Scope validation**
- **B Verification of the interim deliverable**
- **C Managing quality**
- **D Monitoring stakeholder engagement**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Part of monitoring stakeholder engagement is consistently knowing their position on the project.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

Maintaining stakeholder relationships and understanding stakeholders' perceptions of the
project's progress is accomplished in the Monitor Stakeholder Engagement process. Monitor
Stakeholder Engagement is the process of monitoring project stakeholder relationships and
tailoring strategies for engaging stakeholders through modification of engagement strategies and
plans. Meetings, either formal or informal, can be used as a tool in the Monitor Stakeholder
Engagement process. In this scenario, you have had simple conversations with the stakeholders,
revealing their attitudes about the project and its progress.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

- **A Scope validation**
Incorrect. Scope validation is the process of formally accepting a project deliverable.
Before a deliverable can be accepted, it must have gone through the Control Quality
process. In this scenario, the deliverable is in the process of being verified; therefore, it is
not available for scope validation. Aside from that, scope validation is a formal process; it
wouldn't be performed at a barbeque party.
- **B Verification of the interim deliverable**
Incorrect. The Control Quality process determines the correctness of deliverables resulting
in verified deliverables. In the scenario described, the deliverable is in the process of being
evaluated; therefore, it has not yet been verified.
- **C Managing quality**
Incorrect. Managing quality focuses on implementing the quality management plan into
executable quality activities, identifying ineffective processes and causes of poor quality
neither of which are mentioned in the scenario.
- **D Monitoring stakeholder engagement**
Correct. Monitoring stakeholder engagement helps determine the position of stakeholder
groups and individuals at any particular time in the project. The business development
executives, in this scenario, are sharing their satisfaction with the project progress and
interest in the interim deliverable, thereby sharing their levels of engagement.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 533
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 13 of 200
Question ID: 612347
You are managing a site excavation project with an aggressive schedule. You have just received
approval for the project management plan.
Which process are you least likely to perform next?
- **A Execution of the communications management plan**
- **B Selection of the vendors that will produce project deliverables**
- **C Validation of the project deliverables**
- **D Acquisition of the necessary project resources**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Project execution begins after the project management plan has been reviewed and approved by
the relevant stakeholders.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The Project Management Professional (PMP)® Examination Content Outline contains a detailed
list of tasks for each domain, with which PMP aspirants are expected to be familiar. Task #11 of
the planning domain states, "Present the project management plan to the relevant stakeholders
according to applicable policies and procedures in order to obtain approval to proceed with
project execution." Validation of the project deliverables takes place when the Validate Scope
process is carried out. The Validate Scope process is part of the Monitoring and Controlling
Process Group. Since the project management plan has just been approved, proceeding with
project execution rather than with monitoring and controlling makes the more sense. Execution
of the communications management plan, selection of the vendors that will produce project
deliverables, and acquisition of the necessary project resources are all activities that belong to the
processes of the Executing Process Group. Only validation of the project deliverables belongs to
the Monitoring and Controlling Process Group, making that choice the best answer to the
question asked.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Execution of the communications management plan**
Incorrect. Once the project management plan has been reviewed and approved, project
execution can begin. The execution of the communications plan describes the Manage
Communications process which is an execution process, making this choice an incorrect
answer.
- **B Selection of the vendors that will produce project deliverables**
Incorrect. Project execution begins after the project management plan has been reviewed
and approved. The selection of vendors that will produce project deliverables describes the
Conduct Procurements process which is an execution process. Vendors can be selected as
early as project execution begins. Therefore, Conduct Procurements is not the least likely
process to be completed next.
- **C Validation of the project deliverables**
Correct. Validation of the project deliverables is the main activity of the Validate Scope
process. The question states the project management plan has just been approved.
Therefore, it is reasonable to assume that no deliverables have been produced yet, meaning
there is nothing to validate. Thus, of the choices provided, validation of the project
deliverables is the least likely process for you to perform next and is, therefore, the best
answer to the question asked.
- **D Acquisition of the necessary project resources**
Incorrect. After the project management plan has been reviewed and approved, project
execution starts. The acquisition of the necessary project resources describes the Acquire
Resources process which is an execution process, and not the least likely process to be
completed next.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 25; see also Project Management Professional
(PMP)® Examination Content Outline, Project Management Institute Inc., June 2015, Domain 2,
Task 11

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 14 of 200
Question ID: 650108
- **A project manager is leading a product development project, which will use an agile framework.**
The project team and other stakeholders are co-located at the company's corporate office.
What is the best way for the project manager to communicate the project status and promote
transparency?
- **A Reserve a conference room and invite all relevant stakeholders to monthly project status**
meetings
- **B Post burndown charts and other project status documents to the company's intranet site**
- **C Share the appropriate information whenever requested by stakeholders**
- **D Display burndown charts and other relevant project artifacts in a highly visible location**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

How might daily project status updates be communicated using a form of push communications?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

Agile best practices promote transparency. Displaying burndown charts and other relevant
project information in a highly visible location promotes transparency as current information
regarding project status is readily available to everyone. All of the answer choices represent
actions that should be taken by the project manager. The PMP aspirant should select the 'best'
answer among the available options. With the project team and stakeholders co-located at the
corporate office, posting the project status in a highly visible location will make current
information readily available to everyone. Note that the incorrect answer choices all represent an
action that must be taken by the stakeholders in order to retrieve the information rather than
having the information proactively presented to them. The correct answer choice describes an
agile best practice. Therefore, of the available options, displaying burndown charts and other
relevant project artifacts in a highly visible location is the 'best' answer to the question asked.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Reserve a conference room and invite all relevant stakeholders to monthly project status**
meetings
Incorrect. Holding monthly project status meetings is a good idea. However, the project
status will change daily during project execution. A monthly meeting will only provide a
snapshot of the project status. To promote transparency as asked by the question, it is
better to make current information readily available.
- **B Post burndown charts and other project status documents to the company's intranet site**
Incorrect. The project manager probably should post any relevant project status documents
to the company's intranet site. However, this action requires the project team and
stakeholders to proactively access the information rather than having the information
readily available to them.
- **C Share the appropriate information whenever requested by stakeholders**
Incorrect. The project manager should share any relevant information upon request.
However, requiring stakeholders to seek out the information they need is not the best way
to keep stakeholders informed and promote transparency.
- **D Display burndown charts and other relevant project artifacts in a highly visible location**
Correct. Agile best practices encourage transparency. Displaying burndown charts and
other relevant project information in a highly visible location promotes transparency as the
information readily available to everyone.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 365
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 15 of 200
Question ID: 612100
You are concerned that too many quality audits drove the project costs beyond the planned value.
To which cost group would you categorize these audits?
- **A Cost of nonconformance, prevention costs**
- **B Cost of conformance, failure costs**
- **C Cost of nonconformance, cost-benefit costs**
- **D Cost of conformance, appraisal costs**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The work performed as part of the Manage Quality process, which includes quality audits, falls
under the conformance work category in the cost of quality framework.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The cost of quality is divided into the cost of conformance where money is spent during the
project to avoid failures and, the cost of nonconformance where money is spent during and after
the project because of failures. Appraisal costs are a cost of conformance that is related to
evaluation, measuring, auditing, and testing the product or service of the project. Quality audits,
often performed during the Manage Quality process, identify project processes that have gaps or
shortcomings and are, therefore, considered an appraisal cost and part of the cost of
conformance.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Cost of nonconformance, prevention costs**

---

Incorrect. Prevention costs are related to the prevention of poor quality in the products,
deliverables, or services of the specific project. For example, the expenses to cover training
for the team, providing the right equipment, and allowing the team the time to 'do it right.'
Prevention costs are considered the cost of conformance, not the cost of nonconformance.
- **B Cost of conformance, failure costs**
Incorrect. Failure costs are the money spent during and after the project because the
product or service did not meet the expectations of the customer. The scenario does not
describe failures. Also, failure costs are considered the cost of nonconformance, not the
cost of conformance.
- **C Cost of nonconformance, cost-benefit costs**
Incorrect. This answer choice represents a mix of two unrelated items, cost of
nonconformance, which is the money spent during and after the project because of failures;
and cost-benefit analysis, which is a financial tool used to estimate the strengths and
weaknesses of alternatives in order to determine the best alternative in terms of benefits
provided.
- **D Cost of conformance, appraisal costs**
Correct. The cost of conformance is the money spent during a project to avoid failures.
Appraisal costs include expenses related to evaluating, measuring, auditing, and testing the
product or service of the project. Appraisal costs are considered part of the cost of
conformance. Therefore, you should categorize the cost of the quality audits as appraisal
costs and part of the cost of conformance.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 282-283, 289, 294-295
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

Question 16 of 200
Question ID: 613048
- **A new director of business development has just been hired. Recent focus groups revealed**
several promising concepts he is interested in pursuing. But first, he needs to know what projects
are in progress to determine what his involvement should be. The director requests the project
managers in each office send him high-level information on authorized and currently active
projects.
What document would best fulfill the director's request?
- **A Approved business case**
- **B Approved project register**
- **C Approved project management plan**
- **D Approved project charter**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What document contains high-level information about a project?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

When a scenario mentions 'high level,' you should be thinking project charter because it is the
document that contains high-level information about the project. In this case, of the choices
provided, the only answer choice that would provide high-level project information is the
approved project charter. By reviewing the approved project charters, the director would have an
understanding of the key deliverables, milestones, and the role and responsibilities of
stakeholders. He can use the approved project charter to help determine his own role in the
projects.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

- **A Approved business case**
Incorrect. The project's business case is an economic feasibility study demonstrating the
benefits of a project concept and is used as the basis for further project management
activities. The business case would not include the specific high-level information about the
project that the director has requested, and therefore, of the choices provided, is not the
best answer.
- **B Approved project register**
Incorrect. 'Project register' (either approved or not) is a made-up term.
- **C Approved project management plan**
Incorrect. The project management plan is comprised of several subsidiary plans that
describe how the project will be executed, monitored and controlled, and closed. The
project management plan has more project detail than what is being requested by the
director, and since there is another answer that includes a better project overview (i.e., the
approved project charter), the project management plan is not the best answer.
- **D Approved project charter**
Correct. The approved project charter formally authorizes the existence of a project and
provides the project manager with the authority to use company resources. The approved
project charter includes high-level information, such as project objectives, milestones, and
the roles and responsibilities of key stakeholders. The approved project charter would
provide the director with the information he requested.

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 81, 561

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 17 of 200
Question ID: 612977
- **A company is considering two projects, project A with the internal rate of return (IRR) of 25%**
and project B with the IRR of 15%.
Which project should the company select and why?
- **A Project B because a lower IRR represents lower costs**
- **B Project A because it has a higher IRR**
- **C Project B because a lower IRR represents a shorter payback period**
- **D Project A because letter "A" comes before "B"**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The internal rate of return (IRR) is the interest rate at which the cash inflow and cash outflow of
the project equal zero.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The internal rate of return (IRR) is the interest rate at which the cash inflow and cash outflow of
the project equal zero. The IRR can be an important metric for benefits analysis. The PMP exam
will not likely ask you to calculate the IRR. However, two important concepts should be
understood for the exam. First, a positive IRR means a positive rate of return. Second, all other
things being equal or no other details are provided, a project with a higher IRR is typically
selected over a project with a lower IRR. In the scenario described, the company should select
project A with the IRR of 25% over project B with the IRR of 15%.
While the topic of this question is just briefly mentioned in the PMBOK® Guide, the Project
Management Professional (PMP)® Examination Content Outline, June 2015, covers knowledge
and skills with which PMP aspirants are expected to be familiar. Project finance principles are
among these knowledge and skills.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Project B because a lower IRR represents lower costs**
Incorrect. IRR is an internal rate of return. There is no correlation between the IRR and
costs.
- **B Project A because it has a higher IRR**
Correct. The internal rate of return (IRR) is the interest rate at which the cash inflow and
cash outflow of the project equal zero. A higher IRR means a higher potential rate of
growth (return). Therefore, of the two projects, project A with the IRR of 25% is preferable
than project B with the IRR of 15%.
- **C Project B because a lower IRR represents a shorter payback period**
Incorrect. IRR is an internal rate of return. There is no correlation between the IRR and the
payback period.
- **D Project A because letter "A" comes before "B"**
Incorrect. This answer choice is obviously nonsense.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 34-35

Question 18 of 200
Question ID: 612255
- **A project sponsor is developing the project charter. She understands that the project would have**
to take into consideration conditions that are not under the immediate control of the project team.
Which of the following is an example of such conditions?
- **A Project monitoring and reporting methods**
- **B An approved template of a project charter**
- **C Legislation on overtime pay for the project team**
- **D Historical information and lessons learned repository**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Enterprise environmental factors are conditions, not under the immediate control of the team,
that influence, constrain, or direct the project.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The question describes enterprise environmental factors (EEFs), which are conditions, not under
the immediate control of the team, that influence, constrain, or direct the project. These
conditions can be internal and/or external to the performing organization. EEFs are one of the
inputs to the Develop Project Charter process. The legislation, which imposes overtime pay is an
example of a legal requirement which is not under the immediate control of the project team and
is external to the organization. The incorrect answer choices represent organizational process
assets. Among the available options, only the legislation that may impose overtime pay for the
project team represents a constraint that is considered an enterprise environmental factor.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

- **A Project monitoring and reporting methods**
Incorrect. Project monitoring and reporting methods are examples of the organizational
process assets, while the scenario implies the project sponsor is looking for the enterprise
environmental factors.
- **B An approved template of a project charter**
Incorrect. An approved project charter template is an example of an organizational process
asset. Whereas, the question refers to enterprise environmental factors.
- **C Legislation on overtime pay for the project team**
Correct. Legislation that imposes overtime pay is an example of a legal requirement. Legal
and regulatory requirements are enterprise environmental factors, which are not under the
immediate control of the project team.
- **D Historical information and lessons learned repository**
Incorrect. Historical information and lessons learned repository are examples of the
organizational process assets, while according to the scenario, the project sponsor is
interested in the enterprise environmental factors.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 78

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 19 of 200
Question ID: 613794
The total budget for the project is $50 million, and the actual costs so far are $40 million. The
project has a CPI of 0.92 and the SPI of 0.80.
What is the estimate at completion that considers both the cost and schedule performance?
- **A $54.35 million**
- **B $57.94 million**
- **C $53.20 million**
- **D $17.93 million**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Both the SPI and the CPI influence the remaining work, so the EAC formula must be chosen
accordingly.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

In this scenario, the project work that is remaining to be completed is impacted by the fact that
there is no flexibility in the project schedule. The completion date must be met. One needs to use
a formula for the EAC that considers both the SPI and the CPI. This formula is EAC = AC +
[(BAC - EV) / (CPI x SPI)]. The EV is not provided and therefore has to be obtained using the
formula CPI = EV / AC. The details of the calculation are below:
EV = AC x CPI = 40 x 0.92 = 36.8
EAC = AC + [(BAC - EV) / (CPI x SPI)] = 40 + [(50 – 36.8) / (0.92 x 0.8)]= 40 + [13.2 / 0.736]
= 40 + 17.94 = 57.94

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A $54.35 million**
Incorrect. The formula used for this answer is EAC = BAC / CPI. This formula is used
when the CPI is expected to be the same for the remainder of the project. However, in this
scenario, you do not necessarily expect CPI to be the same for the remainder of the project.
Since there is no flexibility on the project completion date, an equation that includes the
SPI must be used.
- **B $57.94 million**
Correct. In this scenario, there is no flexibility on the scheduled completion date.
Therefore, the CPI and SPI influence the remaining work. The correct formula is EAC =
AC+ [(BAC-EV) / (CPI x SPI)].
- **C $53.20 million**
Incorrect. The formula used for this answer is EAC = AC + BAC - EV. This formula is used
when the present cost variance was only a one-time event, and the future work will be
accomplished at the planned rate. In the scenario described, the CPI has been consistently
low, and the SPI needs to be included because the project completion date cannot be
adjusted.
- **D $17.93 million**
Incorrect. The formula used for this answer is ETC = EAC - AC and is the formula for the
estimate 'to' complete, not the estimate 'at' completion. The ETC is the expected cost to
finish all the remaining project work. The EAC is the expected 'total' cost of completing all
project work, which is what is asked for in the question.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 265, 267
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results
Prev Next

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 20 of 200
Question ID: 613773
Increased latency in transaction times was an identified risk for a software upgrade project.
While monitoring project risks, the project team performs some data analysis and discovers that
the latency issues have resulted in average transaction times of 37 minutes versus a target of 12
minutes.
What data analysis tool or technique has the project team most likely utilized?
- **A Monte Carlo simulation**
- **B Multicriteria decision analysis**
- **C Technical performance analysis**
- **D Perform Quantitative Risk Analysis**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What data analysis technique associated with the Monitor Risks process utilizes the technical
performance measurement of transaction times?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The scenario implies the team is carrying out the Monitor Risks process. Technical performance
analysis is an example of the data analysis tools and techniques that can be used as part of this
process. Technical performance analysis compares technical accomplishments during project
execution to the schedule of technical achievement. It requires the definition of objective,
quantifiable measures of technical performance, which can be used to compare actual results
against targets. Such technical performance measures may include weight, transaction times,
number of delivered defects, storage capacity, etc. A deviation can indicate the potential impact
of threats and opportunities. Of the choices provided, based on the circumstances described by
the scenario, technical performance analysis is the most likely tool the project team has utilized.
Note, while "latency in transaction times" may sound like an unfamiliar term, no technical

---

knowledge is required to answer this question correctly.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Monte Carlo simulation**
Incorrect. A Monte Carlo simulation is an analysis technique where a computer model is
iterated many times and outputs are generated to represent the range of possible outcomes
for the project. In this case, the average transaction time has been determined to be 37
minutes rather than a range of possible outcomes.
- **B Multicriteria decision analysis**
Incorrect. Multicriteria decision analysis is a technique that utilizes a decision matrix to
provide a systematic analytical approach for establishing criteria, such as risk levels,
uncertainty, and valuation, to evaluate and rank many ideas. The project team is
comparing the actual project results with the planned targets. This activity is different from
the multicriteria decision analysis making this choice an incorrect answer.
- **C Technical performance analysis**
Correct. Technical performance analysis compares technical accomplishments during
project execution to the schedule of technical achievement. It requires the definition of
objective, quantifiable measures of technical performance, which can be used to compare
actual results against targets. Such technical performance measures may include weight,
transaction times, number of delivered defects, storage capacity, etc. A deviation can
indicate the potential impact of threats and opportunities.
- **D Perform Quantitative Risk Analysis**
Incorrect. Perform Quantitative Risk Analysis is the process of numerically analyzing the
combined effect of identified individual project risks and other sources of uncertainty on
overall project objectives. The question is asking for a tool or technique.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 456
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 21 of 200
Question ID: 612497
You are working with your project team to obtain administrative closure of a project. The project
was performed exclusively with internal resources provided by the functional leaders.
Which of the following is most likely to be the last action taken in this scenario?
- **A Conducting a survey to measure stakeholder satisfaction**
- **B Finalizing open claims**
- **C Transferring the final product to operations**
- **D Releasing the project team**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

At least some of the project team must be available to perform the administrative closure of the
project.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

Although some of the project team members may be released before the project has been closed,
some of the project team must remain to perform the activities associated with the administrative
closure of the project. Even if only the project manager remains on the project, the project
manager is considered a member of the project team. Note, the PMBOK® Guide does not specify
the order in which activities are performed during the Close Project or Phase process. However,
it makes sense that the project team cannot be released until all other activities associated with
the administrative closure of the project have been completed. Hence, of the available choices,
releasing the project team is the last action that should be taken and is, therefore, the best answer
to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

- **A Conducting a survey to measure stakeholder satisfaction**
Incorrect. This answer choice does represent an action associated with the administrative
closure of the project. However, a member of the project team must be available to collect
and analyze the survey information. Therefore, measuring stakeholder satisfaction must be
completed before the project team can be released.
- **B Finalizing open claims**
Incorrect. Finalizing open claims is one of the steps completed during the administrative
closure of the project. Claims may result as part of the procurement process. The question
states that the project was completed exclusively with internal resources, which means that
vendors were not used for the project. Therefore, it is not logical that any claims would
exist in this scenario. Even if the project did have an open claim, this is not the last activity,
of the available options, to be performed.
- **C Transferring the final product to operations**
Incorrect. The transfer of the software to operations is one of the tasks that should be
completed for administrative closure of the project. However, at least some of the project
team must perform this activity. Therefore, the project team cannot be released until this
activity is complete.
- **D Releasing the project team**
Correct. Although some of the project team members may be released before the project
has been closed, some of the project team must remain to perform the activities associated
with the administrative closure of the project.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 121, 123

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 22 of 200
Question ID: 625214
You are leading a project to build ten new houses. This project is the second such for the
company. The previous project came in on budget and schedule. You have been provided the
cost per square foot per home. The same team from the previous project will be working at the
same salary rate on your project.
Based on the information you have, which of the following is the most appropriate cost
estimating tool or technique to use in this scenario?
- **A Three-point estimating**
- **B Vendor bid analysis**
- **C Analogous estimating**
- **D Parametric estimating**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which estimating tool uses both historical data and other project parameters?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

Based on the information provided, you are performing Estimate Costs process. You have access
to the salary of your project team, historical data from the previous similar project, and
information about some of the parameters of your current project. Parametric estimating uses a
statistical relationship between relevant historical data and other variables. For example,
construction projects can use square footage as a parameter. Therefore, parametric estimating,
unlike the other answer choices, is the most appropriate tool to use given the information
provided. Three-point estimating uses a formula that considers three uncertainty and risk factors
in the estimation: most likely, optimistic, and pessimistic. Analogous estimating could also be
used in this scenario, but it is generally used in the absence of current or new information.
Vendor bid analysis involves estimating costs based on bids from multiple vendors.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Three-point estimating**
Incorrect. To define cost range, three-point estimating uses three estimation scenarios:
most likely, optimistic, pessimistic. You are provided the cost elements and are using
historical information as well. Therefore, three-point estimating is not your best choice.
- **B Vendor bid analysis**
Incorrect. Vendor bid analysis would be used by a buyer to evaluate costs of bids from
multiple vendors. The question does not suggest that the project involves multiple vendors.
- **C Analogous estimating**
Incorrect. Analogous estimating uses historical data such as cost and duration from
previous projects to estimate costs of the current project. Analogous estimating is typically
used when there is limited information about the current project. In this scenario, the
information is available, and therefore, analogous estimating is not the best tool for the
project manager to use.
- **D Parametric estimating**
Correct. Parametric estimating is the best technique to use when the information available
about the current project is coupled with the historical information from the previous
project.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 244

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 23 of 200
Question ID: 613417
- **A project manager is nearing the end of a product development project for a large consumer**
goods manufacturer. Several vendors produced key deliverables for the project, and there are no
open claims. The project manager is now carrying out all of the activities associated with project
closure and is following all project management best practices.
Which of the following tasks should the project manager perform?
- **A Close procurements with the vendors**
- **B Formally sign off the project deliverables**
- **C Update the enterprise environmental factors**
- **D Update the organizational process assets**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

How are the finalized project documents and materials archived?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The question indicates that the Close Project or Phase process is underway. During project
closure, the organizational process assets are updated to include finalized project documents,
operational and support documents, project or phase closure documents, and the lessons learned
repository. Therefore, of the available choices, updating the organizational process assets is the
best answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Close procurements with the vendors**

---

Incorrect. Procurements are closed as part of the Control Procurements process, not the
Close Project or Phase process which is, as implied by the question, the process being
carried out in the scenario.
- **B Formally sign off the project deliverables**
Incorrect. Deliverables that meet the acceptance criteria are formally signed off and
approved by the customer or sponsor as part of the Validate Scope process rather than the
Close Project or Phase process. In the Close Project or Phase process, the project
manager 'confirms' the delivery and formal acceptance of the deliverables. While the
difference is subtle, formal acceptance and the confirmation of the acceptance are two
different things. One can think of the confirmation of acceptance as a checkbox that should
be ticked during project closure: "Have the deliverables been formally accepted during the
Validate Scope process?" If Yes, check the box. If No, there is a problem.
- **C Update the enterprise environmental factors**
Incorrect. The question implies the Close Project or Phase process is being carried out in
the scenario. Updates to the enterprise environmental factors are not among the outputs of
this process.
- **D Update the organizational process assets**
Correct. Organizational process assets (OPAs) updates are among the outputs of the Close
Project or Phase process described in the scenario. The updates to the OPAs may include
finalized project documents, operational and support documents, project or phase closure
documents, and the lessons learned repository.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 127-128
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 24 of 200
Question ID: 626019
You are managing a project that encounters many changes. A stakeholder approaches you asking
about the status of a change request that they have recently submitted.
What is your best course of action to address the stakeholder's inquiry?
- **A Consult the project change management plan**
- **B Ask the stakeholder to read the latest project status report**
- **C Consult the project change log**
- **D Send the stakeholder to talk to the project team**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What project document contains the most up-to-date information about the change requests and
their statuses?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

- **A change log is a project document that contains information about changes that occur during the**
project. The change log is updated as new information about a change request becomes available.
For example, if a change request has been approved (or rejected) by the change control board,
the status of this change request should be updated accordingly. It is the project manager's
responsibility to make sure that the information in the change log is up-to-date and
communicated to the stakeholders. Therefore, when asked about the status of a change request,
the project manager should consult the change log and communicate the status to the
stakeholder.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

- **A Consult the project change management plan**
Incorrect. Change management plan is a document that provides information on how
changes will be monitored and controlled. It does not have information about the
individual change requests and their statuses.
- **B Ask the stakeholder to read the latest project status report**
Incorrect. While the project status report may include information about the status of the
change requests, this information may be not up-to-date. From the moment the project
status report has been published, the status of any change request can change. For
example, a change control board has just approved (or rejected) a change request that was
in status 'submitted' in the latest project status report.
- **C Consult the project change log**
Correct. A change log is a project document that stores information about changes that
occur during the project and their statuses. When a project is properly managed, the
changes are logged, and their statuses are updated in a timely manner.
- **D Send the stakeholder to talk to the project team**
Incorrect. Although project team members may know about the status of a change request,
sending the stakeholder to the team will likely interrupt the team's work. Also, the project
team itself is not necessarily involved in executing all approved change requests. It's the
project manager’s responsibility to communicate with the stakeholders and let the team do
their work with as few interruptions as possible.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 120
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

Question 25 of 200
Question ID: 612471
- **A project manager is leading a software upgrade project and is just starting the Plan Stakeholder**
Engagement process. The newest member of the team has limited experience working on
projects and wants to understand the process carried out by the project manager.
How should the project manager respond to the team member?
- **A Communicating with stakeholders to meet their needs, address issues, and foster their**
involvement
- **B Identifying stakeholders and analyzing their interests, influence, and potential impact on**
project success
- **C Monitoring stakeholder relationships and engaging them through the modification of**
strategies and plans
- **D Developing approaches to involve stakeholders based on their needs and potential impact**
on the project
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which response represents an action that takes place during project planning?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

Plan Stakeholder Engagement is the process of developing approaches to involve project
stakeholders, based on their needs, expectations, interests, and potential impact on the project.
The incorrect answer choices are the definitions of the other project management processes
involving stakeholders.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

- **A Communicating with stakeholders to meet their needs, address issues, and foster their**
involvement
Incorrect. This answer choice describes the Manage Stakeholder Engagement process.
- **B Identifying stakeholders and analyzing their interests, influence, and potential impact on**
project success
Incorrect. This answer choice describes the Identify Stakeholders process.
- **C Monitoring stakeholder relationships and engaging them through the modification of**
strategies and plans
Incorrect. This answer choice describes the Monitor Stakeholder Engagement process.
- **D Developing approaches to involve stakeholders based on their needs and potential impact**
on the project
Correct. Plan Stakeholder Engagement is the process of developing approaches to involve
project stakeholders, based on their needs, expectations, interests, and potential impact on
the project. Of the choices provided, this option best describes the Plan Stakeholder
Engagement process and is, therefore, the best answer to the question asked.

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
