PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 51 of 200
Question ID: 612458
During a concept car development project, the leather obtained for the interior was of poor grade
due to an ordering error. The problem was immediately resolved by substituting the low-grade
leather with leather used for the production car line. With the vehicle interior installation
complete, the issue with the low-grade leather will no longer pose a problem for the project.
Based on this scenario, what is the most important action for the project manager to take?
- **A Revise the assumption log**
- **B Record the problem in the risk register**
- **C Inform the project sponsor**
- **D Update the lessons learned register**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The problem described by the question is no longer an issue for the current project but may
affect future projects.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The lessons learned register is a project document used to record knowledge gained during a
project so that it can be used in the current project and entered into the lessons learned
repository. The lessons learned register, as it relates to the Control Resources process, can be
updated with techniques that were effective in managing resource logistics, scrap, utilization of
variances, and corrective actions that were used to respond to resource variances. Although the
lessons learned will be of little value for use on the present project at this point (since the issue
has been resolved), the knowledge gained will be transferred to the lessons learned repository at
the end of the project which will then be available to improve the performance of future projects.

---

Therefore, of the available options, the most important action for the project manager to take at
this point in the project is to update the lessons learned register.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Revise the assumption log**
Incorrect. The assumption log is a document created for the first time as an output from the
Develop Project Charter process to capture high-level strategic operational assumptions
and constraints that are normally identified in the business case before the project is
initiated. The assumption log is then updated as part of the Direct and Manage Project
Work process. The issue has been resolved, and there is nothing in the scenario to suggest
that the assumption log should be revised.
- **B Record the problem in the risk register**
Incorrect. The question does not indicate if the risk of low-grade leather was identified
earlier in the project. Regardless of whether this risk was captured in the risk register or
not, with the interior of the concept vehicle finished, the grade of the leather for the interior
no longer poses a risk for the project. Therefore, recording a risk that has already occurred
is unlikely to be the most important action for the project manager to take in this situation.
- **C Inform the project sponsor**
Incorrect. While informing the project sponsor about the issue and the resolution may be
required, of the choices provided, this action is unlikely to be the most important thing for
the project manager to do at this point.
- **D Update the lessons learned register**
Correct. The lessons learned register, as it relates to the Control Resources process, can be
updated with techniques that were effective in managing resource logistics, scrap,
utilization of variances, and corrective actions that were used to respond to resource
variances. Since the issue has already been resolved, updating the lessons learned register
would be of little value for use on the present project at this point. However, for the future
projects, the knowledge gained during this project will be beneficial. Therefore,
documenting this knowledge in the lessons learned register (to be transferred at the end of
the project to the lessons learned repository) would be the most important action for the
project manager to take and is, therefore, the best answer to the question asked.

**Reference:**


---

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 354, 358

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 52 of 200
Question ID: 612628
- **A business case with a proposal for a project has been submitted to the company's portfolio**
steering committee. The committee approves the proposal and requests one of the company's
project managers to lead the project.
What should the project manager do next?
- **A Meet with the sponsor and key stakeholders to learn the key project elements**
- **B Develop the project management plan**
- **C Determine how to plan for each Project Management Knowledge Area**
- **D Create the project scope statement**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

- **A project charter is developed by identifying summary project information collected from key**
stakeholders.
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

- **A business case is defined as a documented economic feasibility study used to establish the**
validity of the benefits of a selected component lacking sufficient definition and that is used as a
basis for the authorization of further project management activities. An approved business case
serves as an input to the Develop Project Charter process which is the next logical step for the
project manager in the scenario described. However, having an approved business case is not
enough to complete this process. Key project elements and high-level information should be
identified to accomplish this goal. This can be achieved by using tools and techniques applicable
to the Develop Project Charter process. Data gathering and expert judgment are among those
tools and techniques. Meeting with the sponsor, key stakeholders, and other subject matter

---

experts to learn the key project elements from their perspective are examples of data gathering
and expert judgment. Therefore, of the choices provided, meeting with these groups and
individuals is what the project manager should do next.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Meet with the sponsor and key stakeholders to learn the key project elements**
Correct. Since the business case has been approved, the development of the project charter
may begin. By meeting with the sponsor and key stakeholders, the project manager will be
able to identify the project objectives, success criteria, key deliverables, high-level
requirements, and other summary information which will be included in the project
charter. Obtaining these key project elements will assist the project manager in the
development of the project charter, which is the next logical step in the scenario described.
- **B Develop the project management plan**
Incorrect. Based on the scenario described, the project is in initiation. The Develop Project
Management Plan process belongs to the Planning Process Group and can begin only after
the project charter has been developed and approved.
- **C Determine how to plan for each Project Management Knowledge Area**
Incorrect. Planning for each Knowledge Area is another way of saying, 'develop the project
management plan'. To start the development of the project management plan, the project
manager should have an approved project charter first which has not yet been developed.
- **D Create the project scope statement**
Incorrect. The project scope statement is a detailed description of the project scope, major
deliverables, assumptions, and constraints. The project scope statement is developed in
project planning, whereas according to the scenario described the project is still in the
initiation and does not even have an approved project charter.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 75-77, 79-80, 81, 561; see also
https://www.pmi.org/learning/library/concise-project-charter-team-focus-2157

PMP Exam 4

Question 53 of 200
Question ID: 612113
- **A project manager is looking for options to execute some of the Manage Quality activities such**
as failure analysis, design of experiments, and quality improvement.
Which of the following is the best approach for the project manager?
- **A Use the organization's quality assurance department**
- **B Develop a comprehensive communications management plan**
- **C Create the stakeholder engagement assessment matrix**
- **D Involve customer representatives in some of the quality activities**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Quality management is often the responsibility of specific team members.
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

Manage Quality is the process of translating the quality management plan into executable quality
activities that incorporate the organization's quality policies into the project. Depending on the
organizational structure, policies, and procedures, the project manager and project team may use
the organization's quality assurance department, or other organizational functions, to execute
some of those activities. Examples of the activities include but are not limited to failure analysis,
design of experiments, and quality improvement. Quality assurance departments usually have
cross-organizational experience in using quality tools and techniques and are a good resource for
the project. Therefore, of the choices provided, using the organization's quality assurance
department would be the best approach for the project manager.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Use the organization's quality assurance department**
Correct. Depending on the organizational structure, quality assurance departments may
have cross-organizational experience in using quality tools and techniques and are a good
resource for the project to execute some of the Manage Quality activities such as failure
analysis, design of experiments, and quality improvement.
- **B Develop a comprehensive communications management plan**
Incorrect. The communications management plan describes how project communications
will be planned, structured, implemented, and monitored and controlled. In the scenario,
the project manager is looking for options to execute some of the Manage Quality activities
rather than plan communications.
- **C Create the stakeholder engagement assessment matrix**
Incorrect. The stakeholder engagement assessment matrix shows the comparison between
the current engagement level of stakeholders and the desired engagement levels required
for successful project delivery. The matrix is not concerned with the activities related to the
Manage Quality process.
- **D Involve customer representatives in some of the quality activities**
Incorrect. While having the customer involved in project execution may be a good idea
(which is typically a practice used on agile projects by soliciting feedback from the
customer about the deliverables), it is the responsibility of the performing organization to
deliver a product, service, or result and ensure it meets the quality specifications.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 290

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 54 of 200
Question ID: 612132
To test the deliverable, the team is using a testing device, which should be kept in a refrigerator.
Recent test results show excellent precision; however, the accuracy varies with each test run. The
project manager suspects there is a correlation between the testing results and the amount of time
the device has been out of the refrigerator before testing begins.
What is the best course of action for the project manager to confirm or reject her suspicions?
- **A Use control charts**
- **B Use a scatter diagram**
- **C Update the risk repository**
- **D Update the lessons learned register**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

- **A technique used to show a relationship between two variables.**
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The scenario implies that the Manage Quality process is being performed. Scatter diagrams are
an example of a data representation technique that can be used during this process. A scatter
diagram is a graph that tracks two variables to determine their relationship. The scatter diagram
can help decide if there is a relationship, or correlation, between the testing results and the
amount of time the testing device has been out of the refrigerator. For example, the project
manager can plot the dependent variable, the results, on the y-axis of a graph and the
independent variable, the amount of time the testing device has been out of the refrigerator, on
the x-axis. The graph will reveal either a positive correlation, a negative correlation, or no
correlation between the two variables. If the scatter diagram shows any relationship between the

---

testing results and the time the testing device has been out of the refrigerator, the information can
be used to improve the process of testing with the device. Therefore, using a scatter diagram is
the best answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Use control charts**
Incorrect. Control charts are used to determine whether or not a process is stable or has
predictable performance. In other words, control charts can be used to track repetitive
activities to determine whether or not a process is giving results that are accurate and
precise. The project team has already established that the results are precise, but not
always accurate, likely by using control charts. However, the project manager wants to
determine if there is a correlation between two variables, the amount of time the device has
been unrefrigerated before testing, and the results obtained during that testing. Control
charts do not demonstrate a relationship between two variables.
- **B Use a scatter diagram**
Correct. A scatter diagram is a graph that tracks two variables to determine their
relationship. For example, by using a scatter diagram, the project manager can decide if
there is a relationship, or correlation, between the testing results and the amount of time
the device has been out of the refrigerator.
- **C Update the risk repository**
Incorrect. 'Risk repository' is a made up term. Even if this was a real project artifact,
merely updating the 'risk repository' would not help the project manager confirm or reject
her suspicions.
- **D Update the lessons learned register**
Incorrect. The lessons learned register is updated with information on challenges
encountered during the project and how they could have been avoided. At this point, it is
not clear what is causing the inaccuracies. Once the project manager has determined the
root cause of the inaccuracies, the lessons learned register should be updated with the
information so it can be used to improve future performance.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**

---

Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 293
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results
Prev Next

PMP Exam 4

Question 55 of 200
Question ID: 612421
As a project manager, you are planning the kick-off meeting for your current project. A project
team member is assisting you with the arrangements for the meeting and asks you to describe the
purpose of the meeting.
Which of the following is least likely to be correct in response to the team member's question?
- **A Communicate the project objectives to the stakeholders**
- **B Identify the key project deliverables and success criteria**
- **C Gain the commitment of the stakeholders for the project**
- **D Explain the roles and responsibilities of key stakeholders**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

One of the answer choices is associated with a meeting that might be conducted during project
initiation.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The purpose of the project kick-off meeting is to communicate the objectives of the project, gain
the commitment of the project team for the project, and explain the roles and responsibilities of
each stakeholder. Each of these points is captured by the incorrect answer choices. However, the
question is asking to select a response that is the 'least' likely to describe the purpose of the
project kick-off meeting. The identification of the key project deliverables and success criteria
happens during a meeting to develop the project charter rather than a project kick-off meeting,
making the identification of the key project deliverables and success criteria the best answer to
the question asked.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Communicate the project objectives to the stakeholders**
Incorrect. Communicating the objectives of the project is one of the project kick-off
meeting’s objectives., making this choice an incorrect answer.
- **B Identify the key project deliverables and success criteria**
Correct. Identification of the key project deliverables and success criteria are among the
items on the agenda of meetings dedicated to the development of the project charter. Since
the question is asking to select the answer choice which is least likely to be associated with
the kick-off meeting, this choice is the best answer.
- **C Gain the commitment of the stakeholders for the project**
Incorrect. Gaining the commitment of the team and the stakeholders for the project is one
of the purposes of the project kick-off meeting and is, therefore, an incorrect answer.
- **D Explain the roles and responsibilities of key stakeholders**
Incorrect. An explanation of the roles and responsibilities of each stakeholder should be
included in the project kick-off meeting agenda. Therefore, for this negatively worded
question, this choice is an incorrect answer.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 86

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 56 of 200
Question ID: 610083
During project planning, the project team rigorously defined the project scope. During project
execution, a senior engineer calls the project manager and suggests a simpler and more efficient
design which could benefit the project.
What should the project manager do next?
- **A Nothing, no changes are needed since the project scope was rigorously defined**
- **B Discuss the change with the project sponsor**
- **C Evaluate the impact of the proposed change on the project constraints**
- **D Ask that the engineer submit a change request**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The engineer is actually requesting a change. She does it in a verbal conversation. What should
be done first when a change is requested to make sure it's properly handled by those who should
address it?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

- **A change request is a document to record an adjustment to project scope, schedule, cost, etc.**
Changes may include corrective action, preventive action, or defect repair, among others. The
engineer is proposing what she believes to be a valid design change which can be further
evaluated by the change control board. Although changes may be initiated verbally, they should
be recorded in written form and entered into the change management and/or configuration
management system. Thus, of the available choices, asking the engineer to create and submit a
change request is what the project manager should do next, and is, therefore, the best answer to

---

the question asked.
One may argue that evaluating the change should come before submitting the change request.
We had an extensive debate on the subject of change requests in general and on this question in
particular. The reason being is that the PMBOK® Guide does not do a good job in explaining the
exact process in detail. We have discussed this process among our team of certified project
management professionals and have concluded that the first thing that should be done when a
change is requested on a project is the physical creation of the change request, a document if you
wish, filling out a form. Otherwise, on what basis would a project manager and the project team
spend time evaluating a request that is not even documented?

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Nothing, no changes are needed since the project scope was rigorously defined**
Incorrect. Regardless of how much time was spent during project planning and how well
the scope was defined, expecting no changes on a project would be naive thinking. Changes
are normal as project work is performed.
- **B Discuss the change with the project sponsor**
Incorrect. Although discussing the change with the project sponsor may be required at
some point, this action is unlikely to be the next step for the project manager to take.
- **C Evaluate the impact of the proposed change on the project constraints**
Incorrect. While the impact of the proposed change on the project constraints should be
evaluated, the change request should be created first to capture the details and rationale of
the engineer's proposed change request. Otherwise, on what basis would the project
manager and the team spend time evaluating a request that is not even documented?
- **D Ask that the engineer submit a change request**
Correct. A change request is a document to record a change that may affect the competing
project constraints. Given that this change was proposed in a phone call, the change
request will also provide a means to capture the details required to evaluate the impact of
the change to the project.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**

---

Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 115
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results
Prev Next

---

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 57 of 200
Question ID: 612585
- **A project manager is working on a plan for how the project team will acquire goods and services**
from outside of the organization for an infrastructure development project. The project manager
is seeking guidance on what type of contracts can be used on the project.
What is the best course of action for the project manager?
- **A Review the procurement management plan**
- **B Check the lessons learned repository**
- **C Search for the information on the Internet**
- **D Research the organizational process assets**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Where might current procurement policies and procedures for the performing organization be
found?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The question implies that the project manager is conducting the Plan Procurement Management
process and developing the procurement management plan. The procurement management plan
is a component of the project or program management plan that describes how a project team
will acquire goods and services from outside of the performing organization. Organizational
process assets are one of the inputs into the Plan Procurement Management process. The
organizational process assets serve as a source of information on formal procurement policies
and procedures as well as approved contract types. Therefore, of the available choices,
researching the organizational process assets is the best course of action in this scenario.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Review the procurement management plan**
Incorrect. The procurement management plan is a component of the project or program
management plan that describes how a project team will acquire goods and services from
outside of the performing organization. The question implies that the project manager is
developing the procurement management plan. Therefore, the procurement management
plan is not yet available to be used as a resource for information.
- **B Check the lessons learned repository**
Incorrect. The lessons learned repository should be reviewed as it may include information
from past projects that will be beneficial in the development of the procurement
management plan. However, the lessons learned repository will not have the current
policies and procedures regarding contract types.
- **C Search for the information on the Internet**
Incorrect. The Internet may have information on the contract types. However, an Internet
search is not likely to provide current policies and procedures of the performing
organization.
- **D Research the organizational process assets**
Correct. The organizational process assets is a source of information on formal
procurement policies and procedures as well as approved contract types.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 471

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 58 of 200
Question ID: 612584
You are planning a project, where you need several external contractors to complete the project
deliverables. In past projects, internal developers have had disruptive personality conflicts with
contractors. Therefore, before making any long-term commitments, you want to ensure that the
contractors are a good fit for your corporate culture and work well with the internal team.
What is your best course of action?
- **A Send potential contractors to team building workshops**
- **B Conduct a trial engagement with several potential contractors for initial deliverables**
- **C Cover the team charter with the contractors before engaging their services**
- **D Organize a meet and greet with potential contractors and the development team**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

How might the project manager be able to observe how the contractors interact with the internal
project team members in a work setting?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The question suggests that you are developing the procurement management plan as part of the
Plan Procurement Management process. Trial engagements are one of the trends and emerging
practices in procurement management. Conducting a trial engagement will involve several
candidate sellers for initial deliverables and work products on a paid basis before making the full
commitment to a larger portion of the project scope. This engagement may help accelerate
momentum by allowing the buyer to evaluate potential providers, while simultaneously making
progress on project work. The incorrect answer choices are all good ideas that should be
incorporated into the procurement management plan. However, prospective PMP aspirants

---

should always select the 'best' answer among the available options. Conducting a trial
engagement is the best course of action in this scenario.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Send potential contractors to team building workshops**
Incorrect. While team-building workshops may enhance social relations among team
members, it probably would be more effective and useful to send actual teams to team
building activities and training as part of the Develop Team process rather than potential
contractors. In addition, it may not be economically feasible to send all potential
contractors to these workshops.
- **B Conduct a trial engagement with several potential contractors for initial deliverables**
Correct. Conducting a trial engagement will engage several candidate sellers for initial
deliverables and work products on a paid basis before making the full commitment to a
larger portion of the project scope.
- **C Cover the team charter with the contractors before engaging their services**
Incorrect. Covering the team charter with the contractors may provide some future benefits
in avoiding conflict. However, the team charter is most effective when those subjected to its
terms have input into its development. Additionally, just covering the team charter with the
contractors will not provide any insight into how the contractors will interact with the
company's employees.
- **D Organize a meet and greet with potential contractors and the development team**
Incorrect. Holding a meet and greet is a good idea as it will allow potential contractors
and internal employees an opportunity to interact in a social setting. However, a meet and
greet will not provide an opportunity to evaluate how the employees will get along with the
contractors in an actual work environment.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 464

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 59 of 200
Question ID: 612547
While developing a project charter, the project manager recommends using seasoned team
members from key functional areas to assist them in their efforts. She relays to the project
sponsor that input from the seasoned team members would be critical in developing the project
charter.
Which of the following best matches the tool or technique that the project manager describes as
critical?
- **A Analytical techniques**
- **B Project management information system**
- **C Expert judgment**
- **D Meetings**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What tool or technique can be provided by a group or individual with experience in a particular
application area, knowledge area, discipline, industry, etc.?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

In this question, the project manager recommends using seasoned or experienced team members
to utilize their expertise in their particular areas to assist in the development of the project
charter. The implication is that expert judgment from experienced staff in key areas would be
beneficial to the process of developing the project charter. Expert judgment is defined as
judgment provided based on a group or person's expertise in a particular application area,
knowledge area, industry, etc. The group or individual expertise provided can be based on
special education, knowledge, skill, training, or experience. Project managers frequently rely on

---

expert judgment in many project processes to aid in the success of the project. Expert judgment
along with meetings, interpersonal and team skills, and data gathering are all tools and
techniques used in the Develop Project Charter process.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Analytical techniques**
Incorrect. Analytical techniques are various techniques used in data analysis to evaluate,
analyze, or forecast potential outcomes; however, they are not typically used in the
Develop Project Charter process.
- **B Project management information system**
Incorrect. A project management information system (PMIS) provides access to
information technology software tools, as well as interfaces to other online systems such as
corporate knowledge base repositories. Based on the project manager's recommendation of
using input from seasoned team members, the project manager is referring to expert
judgment rather than a PMIS.
- **C Expert judgment**
Correct. The project manager is referring to expert judgment, which is judgment provided
based upon expertise by a group or person in a particular application area, knowledge
area, industry, etc. The expertise can be based on special education, knowledge, skill,
training or as in this question, experience, represented as 'seasoned' team members.
- **D Meetings**
Incorrect. Meetings are a tool and technique in the Develop Project Charter process.
However, the question references to an opinion provided by seasoned team members
(experts). Such an input can be provided at a meeting, over a phone conversation, in an
email, or using any other communication means. There is not enough information in
question to determine if the input has been provided at a meeting. Furthermore, the
question focuses on the source of information (seasoned team members) rather than on the
environment in which this input has been given. Therefore, meetings are the not the best
answer to the question asked.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**

---

Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 79

PMP Exam 4

Question 60 of 200
Question ID: 612188
- **A project manager has just completed the development of the quality management plan and**
determined quality metrics. During this process, the project manager and team identified
numerous quality requirements and standards for the project and its deliverables.
Which of the following would be the most likely outcome of this process?
- **A Updates to the requirements traceability matrix**
- **B Test and evaluation documents**
- **C Determination of the optimal cost of quality**
- **D Project team assignments**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What may be updated as a result of performing the Plan Quality Management process?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

In the scenario, the project manager and team identified numerous quality requirements and
standards for the project and its deliverables. Identifying quality requirements and/or standards
for the project and its deliverables is one of the main goals of the Plan Quality Management
process. The quality management plan and quality metrics are among the outputs of this process.
According to the scenario, the plan and the metrics have been produced. Other outputs of this
process include project document updates, such as the requirements traceability matrix, which is
updated with quality requirements that are determined during the Plan Quality Management
process implied by the scenario. Therefore, of the available choices, updates to the requirements
traceability matrix are the most likely outcome of the process described by the scenario and,

---

thus, the best answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Updates to the requirements traceability matrix**
Correct. The question implies that the Plan Quality Management process is being
performed. The requirements traceability matrix is updated with quality requirements that
are determined during the Plan Quality Management process.
- **B Test and evaluation documents**
Incorrect. Test and evaluation documents are project documents that describe the activities
used to determine if the product meets the quality objectives stated in the quality
management plan. These documents are an output from the Manage Quality process, while
the scenario implies that the Plan Quality Management process is being performed.
- **C Determination of the optimal cost of quality**
Incorrect. The optimal cost of quality (COQ) is one that reflects the appropriate balance
for investing in the cost prevention and appraisal to avoid failure costs. The optimal COQ
is determined using data analysis tools and techniques during the Plan Quality
Management process implied by the scenario, while the question is asking about an output
of this process. Since the quality management plan has already been developed, the optimal
COQ has already been determined.
- **D Project team assignments**
Incorrect. Project team assignments is a project document that records the team members
and their roles and responsibilities for the project. This document is an output of the
Acquire Resources process while the scenario suggests the team is about to complete the
Plan Quality Management process.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 287

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 61 of 200
Question ID: 612418
- **A project manager and team are assigned to a website development project. This project will be**
relatively small, so the same team members will perform the planning and execution of the
project.
When is the best time to conduct a project kick-off meeting in this scenario?
- **A Shortly after project initiation has been completed**
- **B Right before project execution begins**
- **C As part of pre-project work**
- **D During project execution**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The kick-off meeting should occur earlier with a small project compared to a larger project.
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The question describes a relatively small project where the same team members will perform
project planning as well as execution. For small projects, there is usually only one team that
performs the planning and the execution. In this case, the kick-off meeting occurs shortly after
initiation, in the Planning Process Group, because the team is involved in planning. Therefore, of
the available choices, conducting the kick-off meeting just after project initiation is the best
answer to the question asked.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Shortly after project initiation has been completed**
Correct. For small projects, there is usually only one team that performs the planning and
the execution. In this case, the kick-off meeting occurs shortly after initiation, in the
Planning Process Group, because the team is involved in planning. Therefore, conducting
the kick-off meeting just after project initiation is the best answer choice.
- **B Right before project execution begins**
Incorrect. Since the same team members will be involved in planning as well as execution,
it is best to conduct the project kick-off at the start of project planning rather than right
before project execution.
- **C As part of pre-project work**
Incorrect. During pre-project work, the business case and the benefits management plan
are created. The project is not even authorized until the project charter has been drafted
and approved. A kick-off meeting is held to communicate the start of the project, engage
stakeholders, and gain commitment. Communicating the start of the project, engaging
stakeholders, and gaining commitment to the project that has not been authorized does not
make sense.
- **D During project execution**
Incorrect. In this scenario, the same team members will be performing project planning as
well as execution. Therefore, it is best to conduct the kick-off meeting at the start of project
planning rather than during project execution, making this an incorrect response.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 86

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 62 of 200
Question ID: 612461
You and your project team are developing approaches to involve project stakeholders based on
their needs, expectations, interests, and potential impact on the project. To help you with this
process, you have asked a team member to create a stakeholder engagement assessment matrix.
The project team member states that he has never produced a stakeholder engagement
assessment matrix and asks you where to find the stakeholder classifications.
How should you respond?
- **A Conduct interviews with the identified stakeholders to determine their engagement levels**
- **B Perform stakeholder analysis to determine the stakeholder classification levels**
- **C Initial classification information can be obtained from the stakeholder engagement plan**
- **D Check the stakeholder register for the initial classification information**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which project document contains a list of stakeholders along with pertinent information?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The question implies that the Plan Stakeholder Engagement process is underway, and the
stakeholder engagement assessment matrix is a data representation technique that may be used
during this process. Stakeholder analysis is performed during the Identify Stakeholders process
before project planning, and this process identifies stakeholders along with relevant information
including the stakeholders' levels of support for the project. This information is then captured in
the stakeholder register which is used as one of the inputs into the Plan Stakeholder Engagement
process. Therefore, the project manager should advise the team member to check the stakeholder

---

register for the initial classification information.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Conduct interviews with the identified stakeholders to determine their engagement levels**
Incorrect. Interviews with the identified stakeholders might be an effective method of
determining the level of support for the project by stakeholders. However, the initial
stakeholder classification is performed during an earlier process, so the information should
already exist. Therefore, this action is unnecessary and not the best answer to the question
asked.
- **B Perform stakeholder analysis to determine the stakeholder classification levels**
Incorrect. Stakeholder analysis results in a list of stakeholders with relevant information
such as the levels of support for the project. Stakeholder analysis is performed during the
Identify Stakeholders process, which is completed before project planning. Therefore,
conducting stakeholder analysis at this point in the project is redundant, making this not
the best answer choice.
- **C Initial classification information can be obtained from the stakeholder engagement plan**
Incorrect. The description provided by the question indicates that the Plan Stakeholder
Engagement process is being performed. The stakeholder engagement plan is an output of
the Plan Stakeholder Engagement process. Therefore, the stakeholder engagement plan is
not yet available to be used as a resource.
- **D Check the stakeholder register for the initial classification information**
Correct. The stakeholder register contains initial classification information on stakeholders
including the levels of support for the project by stakeholders. Of the available options, this
response represents the best action for the project team member to take.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 519, 521-522

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 63 of 200
Question ID: 612671
You are satisfied with the vendor's deliverables and have sent the vendor the formal written
notice that the contract has been completed.
Which of the following would not be updated during this process?
- **A Procurement file**
- **B Risk report**
- **C Seller performance evaluation documentation**
- **D Lessons learned register**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Closed procurements are an output of the Control Procurements process.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

In this scenario, you have closed the procurements with the vendor; therefore, you are in the
Control Procurements process. The question is asking you to evaluate the answers to determine
which activity is 'not' performed during Control Procurements. Updating the procurement file,
updating the lessons learned register, and completing seller performance evaluation
documentation are all activities that can be performed during the Control Procurements process
making all three of these answer choices incorrect. The risk report, however, is not updated as
part of carrying out the Control Procurements process making the risk report the correct answer.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Procurement file**
Incorrect. The procurement file is a complete set of indexed contract documentation that is
prepared for inclusion with the final project files as part of the Control Procurements
process.
- **B Risk report**
Correct. In the scenario described, you are in the Control Procurements process where
procurements are closed. The correct answer is an activity that is 'not' part of this process.
It is the risk 'register' not the risk 'report' that is updated as part of the Control
Procurements process; therefore, updating the risk report is the correct answer.
- **C Seller performance evaluation documentation**
Incorrect. Seller performance evaluation documentation is prepared by the buyer and rates
how well the seller is currently performing or has performed the project work and is one of
the organizational process assets that can be updated as a result of the Control
Procurements process.
- **D Lessons learned register**
Incorrect. As part of the project documents updates, the lessons learned register can be
updated with techniques that were effective in maintaining the scope, schedule, and cost of
the procured items.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 499-501

PMP Exam 4

Question 64 of 200
Question ID: 610055
One of your contractors is not performing to the agreed-upon standards. You want to terminate
the contract and engage another contractor for the same job. You need to determine the specific
legal procedure for the early termination of the contract.
What should you do?
- **A Check the procurement management plan**
- **B Look at the scope statement**
- **C Review the risk register**
- **D Consult the contract**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What document establishes a legal relationship that is subject to remedy in the courts?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The contract is the document you would refer to in order to understand the early termination
procedure. A contract is a mutually binding agreement that obligates the seller to provide the
specified deliverable. It constitutes a legal relationship. The early termination of a contract is a
special case of the Control Procurements process that can result from an agreement by both
parties, from the default of one party, or for the convenience of the buyer if provided for in the
contract. The rights and responsibilities of the parties in the event of an early termination are
contained in the termination clause of the contract.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Check the procurement management plan**
Incorrect. The procurement management plan describes the project's approach to
procurement, including make or buy decisions. If resources are required from outside the
project, it describes what resources to acquire and how and when to acquire them. The
procurement management plan does not contain specific information regarding the rights
of the seller or the buyer when a contract needs to be terminated.
- **B Look at the scope statement**
Incorrect. The project scope statement describes the project's scope, major deliverables,
assumptions, and constraints. It is part of the scope baseline used to determine the overall
scope of the project.
- **C Review the risk register**
Incorrect. The risk register provides information on threats and opportunities that may
impact project execution.
- **D Consult the contract**
Correct. A properly drafted contract will contain a termination clause that specifies the
rights of the seller or buyer when a contract needs to be terminated.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 489
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

Question 65 of 200
Question ID: 612591
- **A project manager is planning a project to build a new apartment complex on the site of a long-**
abandoned airport that was closed due to illegal dumping of fuel and oil. The project manager
will need to provide a regulatory agency with a detailed explanation of how the cleanup will be
performed before a permit can be issued.
What would be the most appropriate bid document to send to potential vendors for the
environmental cleanup?
- **A Request for information (RFI)**
- **B Request for advisement (RFA)**
- **C Request for proposal (RFP)**
- **D Request for quotation (RFQ)**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which of the bid documents is the most formal and includes a detailed explanation of how the
work will be performed?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The scenario implies the project manager is carrying out the Plan Procurement Management
process. Bid documents are among the outputs of this process. Bid documents are used to solicit
proposals from the prospective sellers. An RFP is used when there is a problem in the project,
and the solution is not easy to determine. This type of bid document is the most formal and has
strict procurement rules for content, timeline, and seller responses. Since the project manager
needs a highly detailed explanation of how the seller will perform the work, the most appropriate

---

bid document to use in this situation is an RFP.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Request for information (RFI)**
Incorrect. An RFI is used when more information on the goods and services to be acquired
is needed from the sellers. While this document may partially address the needs of the
project manager, there is another choice that provides a better answer.
- **B Request for advisement (RFA)**
Incorrect. 'Request for advisement (RFA)' is a fake type of bid document made up for this
question.
- **C Request for proposal (RFP)**
Correct. An RFP is used when there is a problem in the project, and the solution is not easy
to determine. This is the most formal of the bid document types and has strict procurement
rules for content, timeline, and seller responses.
- **D Request for quotation (RFQ)**
Incorrect. An RFQ is commonly used when more information is needed on how vendors
would satisfy the requirements and/or how much it will cost. Although some of the
information the project manager is looking for can be included in the RFQ, another answer
choice more accurately addresses the question asked.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 477

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 66 of 200
Question ID: 651433
An important event indicated in the milestone schedule of a project is approaching when the
project manager realizes that a key stakeholder that was supposed to lead the event is on
vacation.
What did the project manager likely miss?
- **A Canceling the vacations of all stakeholders prior to the start of the project**
- **B Providing the stakeholder with the approved project charter**
- **C Signing a mutually binding agreement with the stakeholder to lead the event**
- **D Submitting a change request to update the stakeholder register**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Where is the milestone schedule documented?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The project charter is the document issued by the project initiator or sponsor that formally
authorizes the existence of the project and provides the project manager with the authority to
apply organizational resources to project activities. Additionally, the project charter includes
high-level information about the project. The milestone schedule, as well as the roles and
responsibilities of the key project stakeholders, are part of the information specified in the
project charter. All identified project stakeholders should be informed of the approved project
charter to ensure a common understanding of the key deliverables, milestones, and their roles
and responsibilities. If the project manager provided the stakeholder with the approved project
charter, the stakeholder would have seen the milestone schedule as well as her role and
responsibility for the event indicated by the schedule and would unlikely have taken the vacation

---

that coincided with the event.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Canceling the vacations of all stakeholders prior to the start of the project**
Incorrect. This action seems extreme and unrealistic, nor is it clear from the scenario if the
project manager even has the authority to cancel the vacations of all stakeholders.
- **B Providing the stakeholder with the approved project charter**
Correct. All identified project stakeholders should be informed of the approved project
charter to ensure a common understanding of the key deliverables, milestones, and their
roles and responsibilities. If the stakeholder saw the milestone schedule as well as her role
and responsibility for the event, it is unlikely that the stakeholder would have taken the
vacation that coincided with the event.
- **C Signing a mutually binding agreement with the stakeholder to lead the event**
Incorrect. A mutually binding agreement is a contract. Contracts are typically used on
projects to oblige the seller to provide the specified product or service or result and obliges
the buyer to pay for it. If the stakeholder were a seller, a contract would have helped
ensure the stakeholder is available. However, it is unclear from the scenario if the
stakeholder is a seller. The way the question is worded implies the stakeholder is likely part
of the performing organization.
- **D Submitting a change request to update the stakeholder register**
Incorrect. Not only a change request is not required to update a project document such as
the stakeholder register, but it is also unclear what change exactly should have been done
in the stakeholder register to avoid the situation described in the scenario.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 81, 561

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 67 of 200
Question ID: 613760
- **A project team is meeting to discuss and assess project risks that have been identified on their**
planned construction project. A facilitator has been brought in to lead the discussion and help the
group determine which risks to prioritize based on their probability and potential impact. During
the discussion, the group identifies additional risks and assigns risk owners to all identified risks.
What technique is being employed in this scenario?
- **A Risk workshop**
- **B Root cause analysis**
- **C Brainstorming**
- **D Risk identification**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What is a technique used in qualitative risk analysis to discuss, analyze, categorize, and prioritize
previously identified risks?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

This scenario closely describes a risk workshop - a technique used to undertake qualitative risk
analysis. The purpose of a risk workshop is to review previously identified project risks, assess
risk probability and impact, categorize and prioritize risks, assign risk owners, and identify
additional risks. Their use of a facilitator was a hint that the project team is conducting a
specialized meeting.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Risk workshop**
Correct. This scenario is an example of a risk workshop - a technique used to undertake
qualitative risk analysis. The purpose of a risk workshop is to review previously identified
project risks, assess risk probability and impact, categorize and prioritize risks, assign risk
owners, and identify additional risks. Facilitators are sometimes used to guide the
discussion.
- **B Root cause analysis**
Incorrect. Root cause analysis is a technique used to determine the basic underlying reason
that causes a variance, defect, or risk. The question does not indicate that this is part of the
group’s discussion.
- **C Brainstorming**
Incorrect. Although brainstorming can be part of a risk workshop, this scenario indicates
that the project team is doing more than just brainstorming. The project team is conducting
a specialized meeting dedicated to reviewing and assessing previously identified risks and
assigning risk owners. Therefore, risk workshop is the better answer.
- **D Risk identification**
Incorrect. Although the project team identified additional risks as part of their discussion,
this is not the primary purpose of their meeting. The scenario states that the project team is
meeting to discuss previously identified risks, which means that the group has already
completed the Identify Risks process and is now undertaking qualitative risk analysis.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 426

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 68 of 200
Question ID: 612359
As the project manager, you are analyzing the project schedule and discover that the project is
behind schedule due to shipment delays and inclement weather. You want to bring current
project performance into alignment with the original planned schedule.
What is your best course of action?
- **A Apply resource leveling**
- **B Adjust the level of effort**
- **C Adjust the leads and lags**
- **D Apply resource smoothing**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Think of ways to refine the project schedule.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

Lead is the amount of time a successor activity can be advanced with respect to a predecessor
activity. Lag is the amount of time a successor activity will be delayed with respect to a
predecessor activity. Adjusting leads and lags is a technique that can be applied in the Control
Schedule process during schedule network analysis to bring activities that are behind schedule
into alignment with the plan. Therefore, of the choices provided, adjusting leads and lags is the
best answer to the question asked.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Apply resource leveling**
Incorrect. When you perform resource leveling, you balance the demand for resources with
the available supply. Resource leveling typically increases the critical path of the project
and, therefore, is not the best course of action to take when the project is already behind
schedule.
- **B Adjust the level of effort**
Incorrect. Level of effort is an activity that does not produce definitive end products and is
measured by the passage of time, such as meetings or administrative work. Level of effort is
not used to adjust the project schedule.
- **C Adjust the leads and lags**
Correct. Adjusting leads and lags is a way to bring project activities that are behind
schedule into alignment with the project plan. Adjusting leads and lags is done as part of
the Control Schedule process while conducting schedule network analysis.
- **D Apply resource smoothing**
Incorrect. When you perform resource smoothing, you adjust the timing of different
activities so that the requirement for resources does not exceed a pre-defined limit.
Resource smoothing is a resource optimization technique and not used to adjust the
project's scheduled timeframe.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 192-193, 214, 228
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results
Prev Next

---

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 69 of 200
Question ID: 612758
- **A project manager is planning a project for his company under a project management office**
(PMO) that can best be described as supportive. The company policy mandates that a change
control board (CCB) must be used for all projects. A project team member shares a draft of the
change management plan with the project manager, which contains the following elements:
• A definition of the roles and responsibilities of the CCB
• A clear description of the process for managing change on the project
• Information on how seller-created changes will be processed
• A list of the stakeholders that are authorized to request changes to the project
What feedback might the project manager provide to the project team member regarding the
draft of the change management plan?
- **A There is no need to specify the roles and responsibilities of the CCB since it is the**
company policy to use CCB for all projects.
- **B Changes can be requested by any stakeholder involved in the project and not be restricted**
to only authorized stakeholders.
- **C Vendors are responsible for producing project deliverables and are not supposed to request**
changes on projects managed by their clients.
- **D There is no need to include a description of the process for managing changes since the**
PMO is available to support projects.
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which element described in the question should not be included in any change management
plan?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

Any stakeholder involved with the project can request a change, and no authorization is required.
It would not make sense to include a list of the stakeholders that are authorized to request

---

changes to the project. The change management plan might assign responsibility to the project
manager, or another team member, for submitting change requests to the CCB to ensure the CCB
is presented with all of the necessary information to render a decision. However, it is not realistic
to restrict stakeholders from making requested changes and would likely be counterproductive.
Of the available choices, stating that changes can be requested by any stakeholder and not be
restricted to only authorized stakeholders is the most appropriate response to the team member
that drafted the change management plan.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A There is no need to specify the roles and responsibilities of the CCB since it is the**
company policy to use CCB for all projects.
Incorrect. Even when a CCB is used for a project, the extent of the authority provided in
the change management plan may vary. For example, the change management plan may
state that all change requests must be reviewed by the CCB or it could state that only
changes affecting the baselines require CCB approval. If a CCB is authorized for a project,
the roles and responsibilities still need to be established in the change management plan.
- **B Changes can be requested by any stakeholder involved in the project and not be restricted**
to only authorized stakeholders.
Correct. Changes may be requested by any stakeholder involved with the project. It would
not make sense to include a list of the stakeholders that are authorized to request changes
to the project.
- **C Vendors are responsible for producing project deliverables and are not supposed to request**
changes on projects managed by their clients.
Incorrect. Vendors may produce project deliverables, but they may also request changes to
the project. The fact the project is managed by their client does not restrict the vendor from
requesting a change when and if necessary. The change management plan should contain
information on how seller-requested changes will be processed.
- **D There is no need to include a description of the process for managing changes since the**
PMO is available to support projects.
Incorrect. A supportive PMO may provide a consultative role to projects by supplying
templates, best practices, training, access to information, and lessons learned from other
projects. A PMO does not eliminate the need for a change management plan.

---


**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 115
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 70 of 200
Question ID: 612189
You are managing a project with four phases and feel the project has completed the work
required to move to the next phase.
What should you do next?
- **A Gather and record any lessons learned in that phase**
- **B Determine the stakeholder roles and responsibilities for the kick-off of the second phase**
- **C Move on to the next project phase**
- **D Gather stakeholders to compare the project and business documents with the project's**
performance
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Phase gates may also be referred to as other terms such as phase review, stage gate, kill point,
and phase entrance or phase exit.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

- **A phase gate, also known as a phase review, is held at the end of a phase. During a phase review,**
the project's performance and progress are compared to project and business documents. These
documents may include the project charter, project management plan, project business case, and
benefits management plan. At the phase gate, a determination is made whether or not to proceed
with the next phase, repeat the current phase (or elements of it), remain in the phase, or end the
project.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Gather and record any lessons learned in that phase**
Incorrect. This response describes a goal of a retrospective or lessons learned meeting and
is not what a project manager should do next if they feel they have completed the work
required of that phase.
- **B Determine the stakeholder roles and responsibilities for the kick-off of the second phase**
Incorrect. This choice describes a kick-off meeting. Kick-off meetings may be conducted at
the start of a project or phase. Before conducting a kickoff for the next phase, something
else should have been done.
- **C Move on to the next project phase**
Incorrect. A determination that the project has successfully met the exit criteria for the
phase must be established before allowing the project to move to the next phase.
- **D Gather stakeholders to compare the project and business documents with the project's**
performance
Correct. This answer describes what happens at a phase review or phase gate to determine
if exit criteria for that phase have been met. Conducting a phase review is the next thing a
project manager should do if they and the team feel all phase requirements have been
satisfied.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 20-21

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 71 of 200
Question ID: 612532
The sponsor asked the project manager to share the project progress and recommunicate project
objectives to the stakeholders. After reviewing the communications management plan and the
stakeholder engagement plan, the project manager decides that a presentation at the upcoming
project status meeting would be the best way to share the information. The presentation is well
received with a lot of positive feedback.
What should the project manager do next?
- **A Update the project communications log**
- **B Update the organizational process assets**
- **C Update the communications management plan**
- **D Update the stakeholder engagement plan**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which answer choice describes an output from the Manage Communications process?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

Organizational process assets (OPAs) are the plans, processes, policies, procedures, and
knowledge bases specific to and used by the organization performing the project. Any artifact,
practice, or knowledge involved in the project is considered an OPA. The scenario suggests the
project is in the Manage Communications process. The communications management plan and
the stakeholder engagement plan are among the inputs to this process. The project manager
reviewed both plans and determined that a presentation at the upcoming project status meeting
would be the best way to share the information with the stakeholders. Updates to the OPAs,
including project reports and presentations, is one of the outputs from the Manage

---

Communications process. The presentation the project manager delivered is considered an OPA.
Since the presentation was a success, a lesson could be learned and used during the remainder of
the project and on future projects. Therefore, the next thing the project manager should do is
update the OPAs with his presentation.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Update the project communications log**
Incorrect. The 'project communications log' is not a term associated with the PMBOK®
Guide. While it is possible that this term is used in the industry, updating the project
communications log (if one existed) would not be the best course of action for the project
manager. Another answer choice better addresses the question asked.
- **B Update the organizational process assets**
Correct. Organizational process assets (OPAs) can be grouped into two categories;
processes, policies, and procedures, and organizational knowledge bases. The OPAs that
fall into the corporate knowledge bases are updated throughout the project with project
information. The presentation that the project manager gave is an example of the type of
information that would be added to the knowledge base aspect of the OPAs. Therefore, the
next thing the project manager should do is update the OPAs with his presentation.
- **C Update the communications management plan**
Incorrect. The communications management plan describes how project communications
will be planned, structured, implemented, and monitored for effectiveness. There is nothing
in the scenario to suggest an update to the communications management plan is required.
The project manager has already reviewed the plan and found that a presentation at the
status meeting was the best way to share the information. Since this approach worked well,
updating the communications management plan is not required.
- **D Update the stakeholder engagement plan**
Incorrect. The stakeholder engagement plan identifies the strategies and actions required
to promote the productive involvement of stakeholders in decision making and execution.
While the presentation may have been identified in the stakeholder engagement plan as an
activity, there is nothing in the scenario to suggest the presentation resulted in a required
update to the plan. The project manager has already reviewed the plan and found that a
presentation at the status meeting was the best way to share the information. This approach
worked well proving the stakeholder engagement plan was adequate and did not require an

---

update.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 388, 39-40

Question 72 of 200
Question ID: 612354
Your project team is located in a building that undergoes renovation. During project execution,
the power goes out. You know that response plans were made in the event of a power outage
which includes the use of a generator, fuel, and an uninterruptible power supply, but you cannot
recall where all these items are located.
What should you do next?
- **A Review the risk register**
- **B Read the risk management plan**
- **C Implement the agreed-upon risk response**
- **D Search any storage areas of the building for the supplies**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Where should you find the agreed-upon risk responses for each individual risk and the nominated
owners for each response plan?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The realized risk described in the scenario should trigger the Implement Risk Responses process.
One of the inputs to the Implement Risk Responses process is the risk register. The risk register
records the agreed-upon risk responses for each individual risk and the nominated owners for
each response plan. After reviewing the information in the risk register, you, as the project
manager, should contact the risk response owner to take the appropriate action outlined in the
risk register. It is reasonable to assume that if planned properly, the risk response specified in the
risk register will have all the necessary details including the location of the supplies needed to
provide the additional power during the outage. Therefore, of the available choices, reviewing

---

the risk register is what you should do next in this scenario.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Review the risk register**
Correct. The risk register records the agreed-upon risk responses for each individual risk
and the nominated owners for each response plan. Therefore, reviewing the risk register is
what should be done next in this scenario.
- **B Read the risk management plan**
Incorrect. The risk management plan describes how risk management activities will be
structured and performed. However, the risk management plan does not have details on
individual risk responses.
- **C Implement the agreed-upon risk response**
Incorrect. As the project manager, you should implement (or have the risk owner to
implement) the agreed-upon risk response; however, the question states that you cannot
recall the details of the response for this risk. Therefore, you should first review the risk
register to find out the details for which you are looking.
- **D Search any storage areas of the building for the supplies**
Incorrect. It is not known from the question whether the supplies are located in the
building, or offsite, or should be delivered by a third party. In fact, it does not matter. First,
you should review the readily available information about this realized risk by examining
the risk register.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 450

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 73 of 200
Question ID: 613670
After completing the process of developing cost estimates for the project, you provide all of the
documentation to the director of finance for review. The following day, the director of finance
calls you with questions on your completed work. She is looking for a range of possible
estimates along with the confidence level of the final estimate, and she cannot find that
information in what you submitted.
What did you likely forget to produce during this process?
- **A Cost management plan**
- **B Three-point estimating**
- **C Cost estimates**
- **D Basis of estimates**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What output of the Estimate Costs process might contain details including a range of possible
estimates along with the confidence level of the final estimate?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The question implies that the Estimate Costs process is being carried out. One output of the
Estimate Costs process is the basis of estimates. The basis of estimates contains additional details
supporting the cost estimate and may include an indication of the range of possible estimates
along with the confidence level of the final estimate. In this case, the basis of estimates was most
likely forgotten during the Estimate Costs process.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Cost management plan**
Incorrect. The cost management plan describes how costs will be planned, but it does not
have details supporting the cost estimates. Additionally, the cost management plan is an
input to the Estimate Costs process and not an output.
- **B Three-point estimating**
Incorrect. Three-point estimating is a technique that uses most likely, optimistic, and
pessimistic cost estimates to define an approximate range for an activity's cost. However,
three-point estimating does not provide a level of confidence associated with the final
estimate. Additionally, three-point estimating is a technique that may be used during the
Estimate Costs process and not an output.
- **C Cost estimates**
Incorrect. The question insinuates that the Estimate Costs process had been performed, and
cost estimates is an output of the process. However, cost estimates will not provide the level
of confidence of the final estimate.
- **D Basis of estimates**
Correct. The basis of estimates is the documentation that contains additional details
supporting the cost estimate and may include an indication of the range of possible
estimates along with the confidence level of the final estimate. Based on the scenario
described, basis of estimates is what you likely forgot to produce.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 247

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 74 of 200
Question ID: 612630
You just received an email from your client stating that as a result of changing government
regulations, the current project is being canceled. You contact your supervisor, who confirms the
news and asks you to terminate the project.
What should you do next?
- **A Release payments to your supplier**
- **B Relieve the project team from their duties**
- **C Identify lessons learned**
- **D Check the termination clause of the contract**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Where would you find information on what your company should do when a project is
terminated prematurely by your client?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

Agreements, or contracts, are an output from the Conduct Procurements process and an input to
the Close Project or Phase process which is, according to the scenario described, you are going to
perform. A termination clause is one of the major components of an agreement. Therefore,
before closing the project, you must first review the contractual rights and obligations with
regard to contract termination and fulfill these obligations. In other words, to ensure that
activities required by the contract are performed when closing the project, you must understand
the termination clause in the contract.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Release payments to your supplier**
Incorrect. While it is reasonable to assume that you should release payments to your
supplier when the project is closed, either as planned or terminated prematurely, the first
thing you should do when a project is terminated is to check the termination clause of the
contract. In the contract, you can determine who is authorized to receive payments, what
portion of the work should be completed for the payments to be released, etc.
- **B Relieve the project team from their duties**
Incorrect. Although as part of the Close Project or Phase process you need to relieve the
project team from their duties, the first thing you should do when a project is terminated is
to check the termination clause of the contract. The project team members may be required
to perform some of the project closure activities. Hence, relieving the team from their
duties may prevent the project from being closed properly and is, therefore, unlikely what
you should do next.
- **C Identify lessons learned**
Incorrect. Identification of lessons learned is done as part of the Close Project or Phase
process. However, this activity is not as urgent as checking the termination clause of the
contract which will determine the next steps to be taken when a project is terminated.
- **D Check the termination clause of the contract**
Correct. When a project is closed, either as planned or terminated prematurely, the Close
Project or Phase process should be performed. However, in this scenario, before closing
the project, you must first understand the termination clause in the contract to decide on
what should be done next.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 489, 123, 128
