PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 100 of 200
Question ID: 612608
To keep stakeholders engaged with and supportive of a project, the project manager wants to
prepare a reporting package to allay their fears on the progress that the project has made thus far.
To prepare this package, the project manager needs to understand the risk appetites and reporting
formats.
What should the project manager do to find this information?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Review the communications management plan
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Look in the risk management plan
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Consult the risk register
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Check the risk repository
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Where are the risk categories, risk appetites, and reporting formats that can be used to manage
stakeholder engagement documented?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The question suggests that the project manager wants to carry out the Manage Stakeholder
Engagement process. The risk management plan is an input to this process and describes the risk
categories, risk appetites, and reporting formats that can be used to manage stakeholder
engagement.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Review the communications management plan
Incorrect. The communications management plan describes the methods, formats, and
technologies used for stakeholder communication. While the communications management
plan provides information on how reporting should be communicated to stakeholders, it
does not provide guidance on risk appetites or reporting formats that can be used to
manage stakeholder engagement.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Look in the risk management plan
Correct. The risk management plan describes the risk categories, risk appetites, and
reporting formats that can be used to manage stakeholder engagement, thus accurately
answering the question asked.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Consult the risk register
Incorrect. The risk register contains a list of identified risks, potential risk owners, and
potential risk responses. The risk register does not provide information on risk appetites or
reporting formats that can be used to manage stakeholder engagement.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Check the risk repository
Incorrect. 'Risk repository' is a fake term made up for this question.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 525

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 101 of 200
Question ID: 612091
- **A current project is much larger in size and complexity compared to the previous projects that**
the project manager has managed. To save time and effort, the project manager uses the risk
management plan and risk register from a historical project as a template. During project
execution, several unexpected high-impact risks were realized, which derailed the project and
caused its termination before completion.
What most likely caused the project to be terminated?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Using templates to create the risk management plan and risk
register
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Failing to implement the agreed-upon risk responses
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Lack of tailoring of the risk management plan and risk register
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Propinquity was too high during project planning
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

How might the project's size and complexity affect the way Project Risk Management processes
are applied?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

Because each project is unique, it is necessary to tailor the way Project Risk Management
processes are applied to a project. Project size and complexity have a direct impact on overall
project risk. A large and complex project requires a more robust risk management plan and a
more detailed risk register to address the increased level of overall project risk. The outcomes of
these tailoring decisions are recorded in the risk management plan. Using the risk management
plan and risk register from a previous project as a template for a larger and more complex project
without tailoring would likely result in the realization of risks without adequate response plans,
which may jeopardize the project's objectives. Therefore, of the available choices, the lack of

---

tailoring of the risk management plan is what most likely caused the project to be terminated
before completion.

**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Using templates to create the risk management plan and
risk register
Incorrect. The use of templates is a project management best practice to save time and
effort. Templates might be found as part of the organizational process assets or derived
from past similar projects. While using templates is an excellent idea, the templates used
for risk management must be tailored to the size and complexity of the project.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Failing to implement the agreed-upon risk responses
Incorrect. The question states that the high-impact risks that were encountered by the
project were unexpected, which suggests that these risks were not previously identified. Any
potential risk responses, which were planned & agreed-upon, were not applicable, as they
pertained to other risks.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Lack of tailoring of the risk management plan and risk
register
Correct. Project size and complexity have a direct impact on overall project risk. A large
and complex project will require a more robust risk management plan and a more detailed
risk register.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Propinquity was too high during project planning
Incorrect. Propinquity is the degree to which the risk is perceived to matter by one or more
stakeholders. High propinquity is more likely to lead to a more robust risk management
plan and more thorough identification of risks along with well-developed risk responses. In
this scenario, the project encountered several unexpected, high-impact risks, which implies
that propinquity was low, not too high, compared to the actual risk faced by the project.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 400
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 102 of 200
Question ID: 613690
You and your project team have just completed defining the scope for your project and are now
in the process of decomposing the scope statement to create the work breakdown structure
(WBS). Some of the deliverables will be produced later in the project and cannot be entirely
decomposed at this time.
When you have completed the process of creating the WBS, your scope baseline will include
which of the following components?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Project scope statement, WBS, and activity attributes
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Project scope statement, WBS, WBS dictionary, and activity list
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Project scope statement, activity list, and activity attributes
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Project scope statement, work packages, and planning packages
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The WBS is created by decomposing the project deliverables into smaller parts. What are these
smaller parts called?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The output of the Create WBS process is the approved version of the scope baseline which
includes a scope statement, WBS, work package, planning package, and WBS dictionary.
Typically, one thinks of a scope baseline as the scope statement, WBS, and WBS dictionary. But
when asked about scope baseline components, one must include the work packages and planning
packages which provide the structure for the control accounts. Scope, budget, and schedule are
integrated and used for performance measurement at management control points called control
accounts which are noted in the WBS. Therefore, the answer that included the work package and
planning package is correct.

---

Note, the correct answer is incomplete. It includes only some of the components of the scope
baseline. However, the incorrect answer choices contain components that are not part of the
scope baseline at all. Therefore, as we always recommend, of the options provided, select the one
that is better than the others even if that option is not an ideal/perfect answer or the answer you
would like to see as the correct one.

**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Project scope statement, WBS, and activity attributes
Incorrect. The project scope statement and WBS are components of the scope baseline,
which is the main output from the Create WBS process described in the scenario. Activity
attributes are an output from the Define Activities process.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Project scope statement, WBS, WBS dictionary, and
activity list
Incorrect. The project scope statement, WBS, and WBS dictionary are components of the
scope baseline, which is the main output from the Create WBS process described in the
scenario. The activity list is an output from the Define Activities process.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Project scope statement, activity list, and activity
attributes
Incorrect. The activity list and activity attributes are outputs of the Define Activities
process, while the question describes the Create WBS process.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Project scope statement, work packages, and planning
packages
Correct. Components of the scope baseline include the project scope statement, WBS, work
packages, planning packages, and WBS dictionary. While this answer choice is incomplete,
of the choices provided, it is still the best answer to the question asked.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 161-162

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 103 of 200
Question ID: 613793
You are managing a project for a grocery store that is upgrading their retail management system.
Your company contracts with a vendor for the supply, installation, and configuration of the point
of sale systems. You have met with the seller to inspect the completed installation of the point of
sale systems and have found they meet the technical and quality requirements outlined in the
contract. The seller has received the final payment.
What should you do next?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Perform a procurement audit
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Close the project
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Provide the seller with formal written notice that the contract has
been completed
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Issue a work performance report
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What is required to close a procurement?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

When a seller has provided the product or service defined by the procurement contract, the
procurement is closed. Requirements for formal procurement closure are usually specified in the
terms and conditions of the agreement and are included in the procurement management plan.
Typically, to close a procurement, all deliverables should have been provided and inspected to
ensure they meet technical and quality requirements, there should be no outstanding claims or
invoices, and all final payments should have been made. In the final step of closing a
procurement contract, the buyer provides the seller with formal written notice that the contract
has been completed.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Perform a procurement audit
Incorrect. Procurement audits are performed during the life of the procurement contract to
ensure the procurement is complying with organizational policies, procedures, and
processes. In this scenario, the contract is in the process of being finalized so an audit
would typically have been done earlier. Therefore, this is an incorrect answer.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Close the project
Incorrect. The contract for the point of sale systems is being finalized. There is no
indication that the entire project is complete. Therefore, closing the project is not the best
answer.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Provide the seller with formal written notice that the
contract has been completed
Correct. In this scenario, you have inspected the completed installation of the point of sale
systems, indicating the procurement is being formally closed. To complete procurement
closure, the buyer provides the seller with formal written notice that the contract has been
completed.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Issue a work performance report
Incorrect. Work performance reports are the organized physical representation of work
performance information. Work performance reports are distributed, as an output from
Monitor and Control Project Work, to stakeholders who need to receive the information. In
this scenario, you are in the process of completing a procurement. Therefore, issuing a
work performance report is not your next step.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 499

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 104 of 200
Question ID: 651438
You are managing a project where several risks have been identified. For low-priority threats,
you decide to forgo the development of risk responses and only establish contingency reserves.
What risk strategy are you using in this situation?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Mitigation
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Acceptance
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Transfer
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Avoidance
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The project manager acknowledges the existence of the threat but does not take proactive action.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The scenario implies you are in the Plan Risk Responses process. Various strategies to address
threats can be used as part of this process, including escalation, avoidance, transference,
mitigation, and acceptance. Risk acceptance acknowledges the existence of a threat, but no
proactive action is taken. Acceptance may be passive, where no action other than monitoring is
involved, or active where an action is taken to handle the risk if it becomes an issue. The most
common active acceptance strategy is to establish a contingency reserve to address the threat if it
occurs. It may be argued that setting aside a contingency reserve is a mitigating activity because
the impact has been factored into the budget. But that is not the same as taking action to reduce
impact or probability. More importantly, establishing contingency reserves for low-priority
threats is exactly what has been described in the question, making acceptance a better choice.
You must always select the best answer and not one that may be or seem correct.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Mitigation
Incorrect. Risk mitigation involves an action being taken to reduce the probability of
occurrence and/or impact of a threat. In the question, you have taken no direct action to
reduce the probability or the impact if the risk occurs. You have simply set aside reserves to
address the impact if the risk becomes an issue. This is not the same as taking steps to
reduce impact like targeting those factors that will reduce the severity of the impact.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Acceptance
Correct. Risk acceptance acknowledges the existence of a threat, but no proactive action is
taken. This strategy may be appropriate for the low-priority threats that are mentioned in
the question. The most common active acceptance strategy is to establish a contingency
reserve to address the threat if it occurs. This is exactly the strategy described in the
question, making acceptance the best answer choice.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Transfer
Incorrect. The transfer involves shifting ownership of a threat to a third party to manage
the risk and to bear the impact if the threat occurs. Nothing in the scenario suggests that
the ownership of the threats has been shifted.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Avoidance
Incorrect. Risk avoidance is a strategy that may be appropriate for high-priority threats
with a high probability of occurrence which would have a large negative impact. The
question describes the strategy for low priority risks which make this answer incorrect
since avoidance is not appropriate for low priority threats.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 443
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results
Prev Next

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 105 of 200
Question ID: 612504
Who can terminate a contract on a project?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Either party before the start of work
BError! Not a valid embedded object.The buyer before the start of work
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Either party by mutual consent
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Early termination is not an option
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Under what circumstances can a contract be changed or terminated?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

Agreements can be amended at any time before contract closure by mutual consent, in
accordance with the change control terms of the agreement. The rights and obligations of both
parties will be captured in the terms and conditions of the contract. The contract terms may or
may not provide circumstances that provide relief from contractual obligations along with any
associated penalties. Without knowing the terms of the agreement, of the choices provided,
contract termination by the mutual consent is the best answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Either party before the start of work
Incorrect. Both parties are bound by the terms of the contract. Unless the contract
specifically states that either party can terminate the contract before the start of work, the
agreement is enforceable. Since the question does not provide any information on the

---

contract terms, this is not the best answer choice.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.The buyer before the start of work
Incorrect. The buyer may be able to terminate the contract before the start of work, but
only if that right is provided in the agreement. The terms of the contract will also outline
any penalties associated with early termination. The question does not provide any
information on an early termination clause which makes another choice a better answer to
the question asked.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Either party by mutual consent
Correct. Agreements can be amended at any time before contract closure by mutual
consent, in accordance with the change control terms of the agreement. If the early
termination clause is not provided in the contract, this clause can be amended by mutual
consent.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Early termination is not an option
Incorrect. Agreements can be amended or terminated by mutual agreement. The contract
terms may also specify other circumstances in which the contract may be terminated before
closure along with any penalties that may be associated with early termination.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 494

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 106 of 200
Question ID: 612479
You are leading a construction project that involves a vendor. A team member tells you that
based on the rough assessment of the vendor's current work in progress, she suspects that the
vendor will be unable to complete their work on time. You share your concerns with the vendor,
but they claim that they are progressing as planned.
What is your best course of action to ensure a mutual understanding of the work in progress?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Conduct a walkthrough
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Perform an earned value analysis (EVA)
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Conduct an audit
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Resort to alternative dispute resolution (ADR)
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

This tool/technique is also called an inspection.
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The question suggests that the Control Procurements process is underway. An inspection, as it
relates to the Control Procurements process, is a structured review of the work being performed
by the vendor. The inspection may involve a simple review of the deliverables or an actual
physical review of the work itself. On a construction project, inspections may involve
walkthroughs of the site by both the buyer and the vendor to ensure a mutual understanding of
the work in progress.
One may argue that the team member has the figures of the work in progress, allowing the
implementation of the earned value analysis (EVA), and, hence, making the EVA a better answer
choice. This is not the case, since, according to the scenario, the team member has only a 'rough'
assessment of the vendor's current work in progress, and she 'suspects' that the vendor will be

---

unable to complete the work on time. Project managers should not act on suspicions. Facts
should be checked, making a walkthrough a better answer.

**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Conduct a walkthrough
Correct. An inspection is a structured review of the work being performed by the vendor.
On a construction project, inspections may involve walkthroughs of the site by both the
buyer and the vendor to ensure a mutual understanding of the work in progress.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Perform an earned value analysis (EVA)
Incorrect. In order to perform an earned value analysis (EVA), you, as the project
manager, must first have a clear understanding of the progress which has been completed.
In this scenario, the status of the work in progress is in dispute and, therefore, is unknown.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Conduct an audit
Incorrect. As they pertain to procurements, audits are a structured review of the
procurement process. According to the scenario, you are concerned with the work in
progress carried out by the vendor rather than with how well the procurement process has
been managed on your project.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Resort to alternative dispute resolution (ADR)
Incorrect. ADR is aimed to address contested changes on projects where the buyer and
seller cannot reach an agreement on compensation for the change or cannot agree that a
change has occurred. Based on the scenario described, resorting to ADR is premature at
this point.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 498

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 107 of 200
Question ID: 612533
Your company's PMO has launched an information dashboard that can be used to share project
communications with stakeholders. The dashboard will display the same information you have
currently been distributing on your project but in a more visual, easy, and quick to read format.
You decide to try the dashboard for communications with a select list of stakeholders.
What should you do next?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Submit a change request to update the stakeholder engagement
plan
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Submit a change request to update the stakeholder register
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Update the communications management plan
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Update the lessons learned register
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What is required to update the project management plan?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The decision to utilize a different tool, technique, method, or strategy, for communication with
stakeholders requires an update to both the communications management plan and the
stakeholder engagement plan. Updates to these plans are among the outputs of the Manage
Communications process described in the scenario. However, before a change can be made to
any component of the project management plan, an approved change request is required. The
change request is key to choosing the correct answer. Ideally, we would like to see an answer
choice of requesting a change request for updates to both the communications management plan
and the stakeholder engagement plan. However, this option is not provided. Two answer choices
partially address the question asked, but neither of them does it thoroughly. Therefore, we have
to select the better of the two options. Of the available choices, submitting a change request to

---

update the stakeholder management plan is the best answer to the question asked because the
solution includes the change request. It is essential to read all the answer options first before
selecting your answer. Sometimes one answer is just a little bit better.
Note, the determination that the project is in execution can be made based on the following part
of the question: "The dashboard will present the same information you have currently been
distributing on your project..." Since the project is in execution, it is assumed that the project
management plan has already been approved and, therefore, any modification to it requires an
approved change request.

**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Submit a change request to update the stakeholder
engagement plan
Correct. Any changes to stakeholder communication strategies and agreed-upon
communication strategies would require an update to the stakeholder engagement plan.
Updating the stakeholder engagement plan requires an approved change request first.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Submit a change request to update the stakeholder
register
Incorrect. You might want to update the stakeholder register to reflect the use of the
dashboard with specific stakeholders. However, the stakeholder register is not a controlled
document (unless stated otherwise in the question) and, therefore, does not require an
approved change request to be updated.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Update the communications management plan
Incorrect. Since you want to make a change to the project communications approach, you
would need to update the communications management plan. However, any change to an
approved project management plan needs to go through the organization's change control
process via a change request. The communications management plan is a component of the
project management plan and, therefore, would require an approved change request before
it can be updated.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Update the lessons learned register
Incorrect. The lessons learned register is a project document that captures knowledge
gained during a project so that it can be beneficial to the remainder of the project. At the
end of the project, the lessons learned register is transferred to the lessons learned
repository for use on future projects. If the use of the dashboard proves to be a better way
to communicate with project stakeholders, this information can be captured in the lessons
learned register. However, since you have not yet proven the dashboard use successful,

---

updating the lessons learned register is premature.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 387

Question 108 of 200
Question ID: 612569
You are leading a project to research, develop, design, and manufacture a new internal
combustion engine. With the design phase complete, it has become evident that the new engine,
although more fuel efficient, is not a viable product due to very high anticipated manufacturing
costs.
What should you do next?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Continue with the project as originally planned
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Submit a change request to update the cost baseline
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Recommend the termination of the project
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Start the Close Project or Phase process.
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The project objectives cannot be met.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The question states that the new engine is not a viable product due to high manufacturing costs.
This situation implies that the project objective of producing a viable product cannot be met.
When the project objectives cannot be met, the best course of action is to terminate the project.
Even though the project should be terminated in this scenario, a project manager lacks the
authority to terminate a project. However, a project manager can recommend the termination of a
project. Therefore, of the available answer choices, recommending the termination of the project
is the best answer to the question asked.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Continue with the project as originally planned
Incorrect. The question indicates that the product under development is not a viable
product. Since the project objectives cannot be met, there is no reason to continue the
project as originally planned.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Submit a change request to update the cost baseline
Incorrect. The question suggests that the project objective of producing a viable product
cannot be met. Increasing the cost baseline will not make the product competitive in the
marketplace. Therefore, there is no reason to continue spending company resources to
develop the product further.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Recommend the termination of the project
Correct. This situation implies that the project objective of producing a viable product
cannot be met. When the project objectives cannot be met, the best course of action is to
terminate the project.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Start the Close Project or Phase process.
Incorrect. The project will likely be terminated in this scenario, which will then trigger the
Close Project or Phase process. However, a project manager cannot terminate the project
and start the Close Project or Phase process without prior authorization.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 5, 542

Question 109 of 200
Question ID: 613104
- **A project manager is assigned to a research and development project for an external client and is**
currently in the process of developing a list of potential stakeholders. The project is still in the
initiation stage, and the project charter has yet to be approved. The project manager has already
reviewed an early draft of the project charter and consulted the business documents to find
potential stakeholders.
What else might the project manager do to identify stakeholders?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Look at the stakeholder register
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Review the contract
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Research the business case
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Read the stakeholder engagement plan
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What source of information regarding the identification of stakeholders is available at the stage
of the project described by the question?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The question implies that the initial pass of the Identify Stakeholders is being performed. The
question also indicates that the project is being undertaken for the benefit of an external client.
As such, a contract should be in place which defines the agreement between the performing
organization and the client. The parties to the agreement are project stakeholders, and the
agreement may contain references to additional stakeholders. The incorrect answer choices
represent sources of information that have already been reviewed or have not yet been developed
at the initiation stage of the project. Therefore, of the available choices, reviewing the contract is
the best answer to the question asked.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Look at the stakeholder register
Incorrect. The question implies that the project manager is performing the initial pass of
the Identify Stakeholders process. The stakeholder register is the main output of the Identify
Stakeholders process. The stakeholder register does not exist until the Identify Stakeholder
process is complete and is not yet available to serve as a source of information.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Review the contract
Correct. The question indicates that the project is being undertaken for an external client.
As such, a contract should be in place which defines the agreement between the performing
organization and the client. The parties to the agreement are project stakeholders, and the
agreement may contain references to additional stakeholders.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Research the business case
Incorrect. The business documents include the business case and the benefits management
plan. The question states that the project manager has already reviewed the business
documents and the business case by extension. Therefore, researching the business case
would be a redundant and unnecessary activity.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Read the stakeholder engagement plan
Incorrect. The question states that the project charter has yet to be approved. Project
planning cannot begin until the project charter has been approved by the project sponsor.
The stakeholder engagement plan is a component of the project management plan and is
developed during the planning stage of the project. Therefore, the stakeholder engagement
plan does not yet exist to serve as a source of information for identifying stakeholders.

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 110 of 200
Question ID: 613128
You are leading a project to renovate and convert a historic building into condominiums. After
some demolition, asbestos insulation was discovered. This came as a surprise to the project team.
To address the issue, the team recommends some scope changes. However, with the cost of these
changes, the budget at completion cannot be met. A change request has been submitted and
approved.
What should you do next?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Update the cost baseline as outlined in the approved change
request
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Use contingency reserves allocated for the risk of asbestos
insulation
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Terminate the project since original project objectives cannot be
met
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Do not implement the change and proceed as originally planned
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The project budget includes the management reserves and cost baseline.
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The scenario describes an unknown risk that requires changes in scope. In other words, the
scenario suggests that the Control Scope process is being carried out. Various components of the
project management plan may be updated as a result of this process. The cost baseline is one of
them. Changes to the cost baseline are incorporated in response to approved changes in scope,
resources, or cost estimates. In this case, scope changes recommended by the team have been
approved. The question does not describe all of the changes which were requested. However, at a
minimum, and with the given set of the answer choices, the cost baseline must be updated since

---

the question specifically states that the original budget at completion cannot be met. Therefore,
of the available choices, updating the cost baseline as outlined by the approved change request is
what you, as the project manager should do next.

**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Update the cost baseline as outlined in the approved
change request
Correct. The question does not describe all of the changes which were requested. However,
at a minimum, the cost baseline must be updated since the question states that the original
budget was no longer attainable.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Use contingency reserves allocated for the risk of
asbestos insulation
Incorrect. Contingency reserves are allocated for identified risks. According to the
scenario, asbestos insulation came as a surprise to the project team, implying this risk has
not been identified earlier in the project, and therefore no contingency reserves have been
allocated.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Terminate the project since original project objectives
cannot be met
Incorrect. The question states that the resulting change request was approved. Therefore,
the project will proceed with a new cost baseline as well as any other approved changes.
Additionally, you, as a project manager, does not have the authority to terminate a project.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Do not implement the change and proceed as originally
planned
Incorrect. While not every change must be immediately implemented, proceeding as
originally planned under the circumstances described in the scenario may be perceived as
simply ignoring the issue. The change has been submitted, project resources have been
spent to evaluate and decide on the change. The change request was eventually approved.
The next logical step for the project manager would be implementing the change rather
than proceeding with the project as originally planned.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 171
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 111 of 200
Question ID: 612127
- **A project manager suspects that duplicate testing performed by one of the company's**
departments is why the project is behind schedule. The department manager explains that two
testing cycles are departmental policy to ensure the highest quality possible.
What should the project manager do to find the reason for the project to fall behind schedule?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Do nothing and let the department continue with their practice
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Perform data analysis using an Ishikawa diagram
CError! Not a valid embedded object.File a formal complaint to the project management office (PMO)
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Adjust the project schedule to reflect the delays
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The project manager should look for the root cause of the issue so that it can be corrected.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The project manager's conversation with the department manager suggests the possible cause for
the department's slow progress is the duplicate testing policy; however, it is just an assumption.
The project manager needs to be proactive and take action. An Ishikawa diagram, which can be
used for data analysis, is also known as a cause-and-effect diagram, fishbone diagram, or why-
why diagram. This type of diagram breaks down the causes of the problem statement into
discrete branches, e.g., activities taking longer than planned, helping to identify the primary or
root cause of the problem. Using an Ishikawa diagram will help determine the real root cause for
the project to fall behind schedule. This could be the duplicate testing or something else. The
root cause analysis will help determine the real underlying reason and enable the project manager
to make an informed decision on what actions are required to fix the problem.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Do nothing and let the department continue with their
practice
Incorrect. Doing nothing and letting the department continue their practice of duplicate
testing will likely keep the project behind schedule. At this point, the project manager
'suspects' the duplicate testing is the cause of the project delay. To confirm (or reject) this
suspicion, an analysis should be made.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Perform data analysis using an Ishikawa diagram
Correct. A good project manager is proactive and should look for a root cause and solution
for a problem even if it means trying to improve another department's processes. An
Ishikawa or cause-and-effect diagram can be used to identify the root cause of the
department's slow progress. The schedule delay may or may not be due to the duplicate
testing being done by that department.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.File a formal complaint to the project management
office (PMO)
Incorrect. First, it is unclear what role (supportive, controlling, or directive) does the PMO
play in the organization. Second, regardless of the role, filing a complaint (either formal or
informal) does not sound like a reasonable action or an acceptable project management
practice under the circumstances described by the scenario.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Adjust the project schedule to reflect the delays
Incorrect. Merely adjusting the schedule would not help the project manager determine the
real reason for why the project is behind schedule. The project manager should look for the
root cause of the problem and attempt to fix it, rather than react and adjust the schedule.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 293
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 112 of 200
Question ID: 612488
- **A project manager is leading a project in which a vendor was engaged under a time and materials**
contract. During a procurement audit, it was discovered that the vendor had been using ghost
employees to inflate the cost of the project artificially. As a result, the vendor was terminated for
cause.
Which organizational process asset is updated to ensure the vendor will not be allowed to work
on future projects?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Procurement management plan
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Procurement file
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Lessons learned register
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Seller performance evaluation documentation
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Not all of the available options are organizational process assets.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

Of the available options, only the procurement file and the seller performance evaluation
documentation are organizational process assets. Seller performance evaluation documentation is
prepared by the buyer and documents the seller's ability to continue to perform work on the
current contract, indicates whether the seller can be allowed to perform work on future projects,
or rates how well the seller is performing the project work or has performed in the past.
Additionally, if the vendor was listed as a preapproved seller, then the prequalified seller list
should be updated to remove the vendor from being preapproved for future work, but the
prequalified seller list was not listed as an answer choice. Therefore, of the choices provided,
seller performance evaluation documentation is the best answer to the question asked.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Procurement management plan
Incorrect. The procurement management plan is not updated with performance issues of
vendors. Additionally, the procurement management plan is a component of the project
management plan and not an organizational process asset.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Procurement file
Incorrect. The procurement file contains a complete set of indexed contract documentation.
While the procurement file is an organizational process asset, it does not include
information on seller performance, and, therefore, is not the best answer to the question
asked.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Lessons learned register
Incorrect. The lessons learned register might be updated with details on issues encountered
during a procurement audit. However, the lessons learned register is a project document
and not an organizational process asset.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Seller performance evaluation documentation
Correct. Seller performance evaluation documentation is prepared by the buyer and
documents the seller's ability to continue to perform work on the current contract, indicates
whether the seller can be allowed to perform work on future projects, or rates how well the
seller is performing the project work or has performed in the past. Also, the question
implies that the Control Procurements process is carried out in the scenario, and seller
performance evaluation documentation is one of the organizational process assets that may
be updated during that process.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 501

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 113 of 200
Question ID: 613025
- **A project manager is performing the activities required to close the project. Although the**
stakeholders are pleased with the results of the project, there were quite a few missteps along the
way, and the project manager and team learned a great deal. The project manager wants to ensure
that the knowledge gained from this project can benefit future projects.
What should the project manager do first?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Finalize the lessons learned register
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Meet with the project managers of future projects and share the
knowledge
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Prepare the final project report
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Hand over the lessons learned register to the project
management office
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

All of the project documents are updated to their final versions during the Close Project or Phase
process.
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The question suggests that the Close Project or Phase process is being performed. During the
Close Project or Phase process, all of the project documents, including the lessons learned
register, are updated to their final versions. The lessons learned register is a project document
used to record knowledge gained during a project so that it can be used in the current project and
entered into the lessons learned repository as part of the Close Project or Phase process. The
lessons learned repository is an organizational process asset, which serves as a store of historical
information about lessons learned from projects. The lessons learned register should first be
finalized before the information is transferred to the lessons learned repository where it will be

---

available for use on future projects.

**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Finalize the lessons learned register
Correct. The lessons learned from the project should be finalized before being entered into
the lessons learned repository.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Meet with the project managers of future projects and
share the knowledge
Incorrect. While a meeting can be a good idea, it is unrealistic to assume that one can meet
with the project managers of all future projects. There is another, more efficient and formal
way of ensuring that the knowledge gained from this project can benefit future projects.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Prepare the final project report
Incorrect. The final project report is prepared as part of the Close Project or Phase
process. However, the question is asking about how knowledge gained during the project is
made available for use in future projects. The final project report provides a summary of
project performance rather than knowledge gained during the project.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Hand over the lessons learned register to the project
management office
Incorrect. The project management office (PMO) is an organizational structure that
standardizes the project-related governance processes and facilitates the sharing of
resources, methodologies, tools, and techniques. Sharing the knowledge gained from one
project to benefit future projects is not among the responsibilities of the PMO.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 124

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 114 of 200
Question ID: 613720
You are a project manager conducting a meeting with your newly hired project team. The
primary purpose of the meeting is to assign roles and responsibilities to the team members. Since
the team members are meeting for the first time, you have each of them introduce themselves
and participate in a team-building exercise.
What stage in the Tuckman ladder model of team development does this scenario represent?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Norming
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Forming
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Initiating
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Mourning
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What stage of the Tuckman ladder model of team development is represented by team members
meeting for the first time?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The question is referring to the Tuckman ladder of team development. The question describes a
meeting where the team is meeting for the first time. The forming phase is where team members
meet and learn about the project and their formal roles and responsibilities. The forming phase is
the stage of team development that is described by the question.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Norming
Incorrect. In the norming phase, team members begin to work together and adjust their
work habits and behaviors to support the team. The team members learn to trust each
other. The question states that the team members are meeting for the first time, and
therefore have yet to have the opportunity to adjust their work habits and behaviors.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Forming
Correct. The forming phase is where team members meet and learn about the project and
their formal roles and responsibilities. The forming phase is the stage of team development
that is described by the question.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Initiating
Incorrect. 'Initiating' is not one of the five stages identified in the Tuckman ladder model of
team development.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Mourning
Incorrect. The mourning phase is also referred to as the adjourning phase. In this phase,
the team completes the work and moves on from the project. The question describes a team
meeting for the first time rather than a team at the completion of a project.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 338

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 115 of 200
Question ID: 612720
- **A project manager has been chosen to lead the project to find a location for a second**
headquarters. The project manager wants to formalize the authority that has been assigned to her
and to gain commitment and acceptance for the project.
What is the best thing for the project manager to do?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Inform stakeholders of the approved project charter
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Obtain project charter approval from the sponsor
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Propose an implementation approach
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Meet with relevant stakeholders to determine the feasibility of
the project
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What is the primary reason for a project charter?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

An approved project charter formally authorizes the existence of a project and provides the
project manager with the authority to apply organizational resources to project activities.
Therefore, if the project manager wants to formalize the authority assigned to her and gain
commitment and acceptance for the project, the best thing for the project manager to do of the
choices provided is to obtain approval for the project charter from the sponsor.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Inform stakeholders of the approved project charter
Incorrect. The scenario states that the project manager wants to formalize the authority
that has been assigned to her implying that the authority has not yet been formalized, i.e.,
the project charter has not yet been approved. If the charter has not yet been approved,
there is nothing to inform the stakeholders about.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Obtain project charter approval from the sponsor
Correct. An approved project charter is a document that formally authorizes the existence
of a project and provides the project manager with the authority to apply organizational
resources to project activities. One of the benefits of an approved charter is that it shows
the company's commitment and acceptance of the project. Therefore, obtaining project
charter approval is the best way for the project manager to formalize the authority that has
been given to her.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Propose an implementation approach
Incorrect. An implementation approach based on high-level risks, assumptions, and
constraints established on the current environment, organizational factors, and historical
data may be proposed as part of the business case. The implementation approach will not
formalize the project manager's authority on the project and therefore is not the best
answer.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Meet with relevant stakeholders to determine the
feasibility of the project
Incorrect. According to the scenario, the project manager has been chosen as the project
manager of the project. This suggests the feasibility of the project has already been
decided, and the project has been justified.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 75; see also Project Management Professional
(PMP)® Examination Content Outline, June 2015, Project Management Institute, Inc., Domain I,
Task 6

Question 116 of 200
Question ID: 613663
The project sponsor asks for an estimate of when the project will be complete. In response to this
request, the project manager performs a calculation and determines that the project has an SPI of
1.1. Based on this information, the project manager creates an updated timeline and tells the
sponsor that the project is estimated to be completed one week ahead of schedule.
What has the project manager provided to the project sponsor?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Work performance information
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Schedule baseline
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Milestone schedule
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Schedule forecast
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What does an estimated or predicted completion date represent?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The question suggests that the project manager is carrying out the Control Schedule process.
Work performance information and schedule forecasts are two outputs of the Control Schedule
process. The SPI of 1.1 provided in the question is an example of work performance information.
Schedule forecasts are estimates or predictions of conditions and events in the project’s future
based on information and knowledge available at the time the schedule is calculated. A schedule
forecast was made based upon the SPI of 1.1 and then provided to the project sponsor.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Work performance information
Incorrect. The SPI of 1.1 is an example of work performance information. However, the
project manager provided the sponsor with a schedule forecast and not the work
performance information.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Schedule baseline
Incorrect. The schedule baseline is the approved version of the schedule, as opposed to the
forecasted completion date provided by the project manager.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Milestone schedule
Incorrect. A milestone schedule is a type of schedule that presents milestones with planned
dates. The project manager gave the sponsor an estimated completion date and not the
planned date.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Schedule forecast
Correct. Schedule forecasts are estimates or predictions of conditions and events in the
project’s future based on information and knowledge available at the time the schedule is
calculated. A schedule forecast was made based upon the SPI of 1.1 and provided to the
project sponsor.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 228

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 117 of 200
Question ID: 613736
The project manager is 6 months into a multi-million-dollar project. The latest analysis shows a
CPI of 1.5 and an SPI of 0.6.
What should she do?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Nothing. The analysis shows the project is on budget and on
schedule.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Consider crashing the project
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Replace one of the higher paid team members with a lower-
salaried employee
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Inform the customer that you are extending the delivery date for
the project
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

An SPI of 0.6 and a CPI of 1.5 mean the project is behind schedule and under budget.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

Earned value analysis is used in a project to compare planned versus actual schedule
performance and planned versus actual cost performance to decide whether a corrective or
preventive action is required. A CPI of 1.5 means that the project is getting $1.50 worth of work
out of every $1.00 spent. Therefore, the project is under budget, and no corrective or
preventive action is required. An SPI of 0.6 means that the project is only progressing at 60% of
the rate originally planned. Therefore, the project is behind schedule, and corrective action is
required. Since the project is under budget, there is funding to bring additional team members in
or crash the project.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Nothing. The analysis shows the project is on budget
and on schedule.
Incorrect. The analysis given in the scenario says the CPI is 1.5; meaning the project is
getting $1.50 worth of work for every $1.00 spent or the project is under budget. The SPI
mentioned in the scenario is 0.6, meaning the project is only progressing at 60% of the rate
planned or the project is behind schedule. The project manager should look for options to
correct the schedule. Therefore, doing nothing is not the right answer.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Consider crashing the project
Correct. Crashing the project is a technique used to shorten the project schedule by adding
members to the team. With a CPI of 1.5, the project is under budget; therefore, adding
additional team members is a viable option for bringing the project schedule back into
alignment with the schedule baseline.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Replace one of the higher paid team members with a
lower-salaried employee
Incorrect. The scenario describes a project that is under budget with a CPI of 1.5, and
behind schedule with an SPI of 0.6. Replacing a higher paid team member with a lower
salaried one would not improve the schedule, which is the problem. Therefore, this is an
incorrect answer.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Inform the customer that you are extending the delivery
date for the project
Incorrect. Earned value analysis is used in a project to compare planned versus actual
schedule performance and decide whether a corrective or preventive action is required.
The project manager cannot arbitrarily adjust the schedule baseline. Therefore, this is not
a correct answer.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 215, 228, 261-262
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results
Prev Next

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 118 of 200
Question ID: 612136
Project communications have not been well received. While the technical stakeholders are
satisfied with the content of the reports, the human resources stakeholders feel that the content is
too technical and therefore do not read the reports.
What aspect of planning communications was missed during the development of the
communications approach for the project?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Sensitivity and confidentiality of the project information
BError! Not a valid embedded object.The method used to distribute project communications
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Which stakeholders wield power
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Awareness of cultural and personal differences
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The answer represents an interpersonal and team skill.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

Cultural awareness is an example of interpersonal and team skills that can be used among the
tools and techniques during the Plan Communications Management process. Cultural awareness
is an understanding of the differences between individuals or groups and adapting the project's
communication strategy accordingly. Culture is often thought of as describing differences in
nationality, ethnicity, or race. However, culture can also be used to describe differences in
professional discipline. People from different professional disciplines may communicate using
different languages, for example, members of technical departments may use more technical
descriptions or words specific to their fields which will likely be too technical to the members of
the human resource department. In the scenario, the communication issues seem to be related to
the technical content. The project manager should have been more aware of the cultural

---

differences within the stakeholder community and adjusted the communications accordingly.

**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Sensitivity and confidentiality of the project information
Incorrect. The scenario suggests the problem with the project communications are related
to content and not the confidentiality of the information.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.The method used to distribute project communications
Incorrect. In the scenario, the issue with the project communications appears to be related
to the content of the communications and not the method used to distribute the reports.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Which stakeholders wield power
Incorrect. Understanding which stakeholders wield power is part of political awareness.
Using the interpersonal skill of political awareness helps the project manager plan
communications based on the project environment as well as the organization’s political
environment. The question does not provide enough information to determine if any power
relationships exist within the stakeholders' community. Therefore, it cannot be assumed
that the political awareness aspect of communications planning was missed.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Awareness of cultural and personal differences
Correct. Cultural awareness is an understanding of the differences between individuals or
groups and adapting the project's communication strategy accordingly. People from
different professional disciplines represent different cultures and therefore, may require a
different type of communications. The project manager should have been more aware of the
cultural differences within the stakeholder community and adjusted the communications
accordingly.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 376, 373
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 119 of 200
Question ID: 612462
- **A project requires the use of various contractors to complete the project deliverables, and you**
have scheduled a bidder conference as part of the procurement process.
Which of the following values is best represented by holding a bidder conference?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Responsibility
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Honesty
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Respect
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Fairness
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

- **A bidder conference is used to ensure that all potential bidders have a clear and common**
understanding of the procurement and no bidders receive preferential treatment.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

- **A bidder conference is a meeting between the buyer and prospective sellers before proposal**
submittal. They are used to ensure that all potential bidders have a clear and common
understanding of the procurement and no bidders receive preferential treatment. Of the available
choices, providing equal access to information best exemplifies the value of fairness.

**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Responsibility
Incorrect. Responsibility is a duty to take ownership of the decisions one makes or fails to

---

make, the actions one takes or fails to take, and the consequences that result. A bidder
conference does not directly promote taking ownership of actions or decisions.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Honesty
Incorrect. Honesty is a duty to understand the truth and act truthfully both in
communications and in conduct. A bidder conference provides equal access to information
but is not directly related to honest communications or conduct.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Respect
Incorrect. Respect is a duty to show high regard for the entrusted resources. These
resources may include people, money, reputation, the safety of others, and natural or
environmental resources. Although holding a bidder conference does convey respect to the
prospective bidders, the primary purpose of a bidder conference is to provide a clear and
common understanding and ensure that no bidders receive preferential treatment.
Therefore, of the available options, respect is not the best answer to the question asked.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Fairness
Correct. A bidder conference is used to ensure that all potential bidders have a clear and
common understanding of the procurement and no bidders receive preferential treatment.
Providing equal access to information is an example of the value of fairness.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 487; see also The PMI Code of Ethics and
Professional Conduct, Fairness

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 120 of 200
Question ID: 612121
To promote continuous improvement, your organization uses a methodology that involves
defining the objectives and scope of the project, measuring to obtain data, analyzing the collected
data to find the root causes, improving by developing a solution, and controlling by evaluating
the implemented solution.
What quality improvement method is your organization using?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Total Quality Management (TQM)
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Six Sigma
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Quality function deployment (QFD)
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Deming's PDCA cycle
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

One of the most common quality improvement tools used to analyze and evaluate opportunities
for improvement.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The Six Sigma method of quality improvement focuses on increasing the effectiveness and
efficiencies of projects and eliminating defects and waste. The Six Sigma method is more
comprehensive than prior process improvement initiatives such as Total Quality Management
(TQM) and Continuous Quality Improvement (CQI). The scenario describes the steps in the
methodology currently in place in your organization. Those steps are the phases of Six Sigma:
Define: The objectives and scope of the project are defined. Relevant information about the
process and customer are collected.

---

Measure: Data on the current situation and process metrics are collected.
Analyze: Collected data are analyzed to find the root cause(s) of the problem.
Improve: Solution(s) to the problem are developed and implemented.
Control: The implemented solution(s) are evaluated, and mechanisms are implemented to hold
the gains, which may include standardization.
Therefore, based on the description of these steps, the quality improvement method your
organization uses is Six Sigma.
While the topic of this question is not included in the PMBOK® Guide, the Project Management
Professional (PMP)® Examination Content Outline, June 2015, covers knowledge and skills,
such as continuous improvement processes, with which PMP aspirants are expected to be
familiar. Six Sigma is one of these topics.

**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Total Quality Management (TQM)
Incorrect. TQM describes a management approach to long-term success through customer
satisfaction. In a TQM effort, all members of an organization participate in improving
processes, products, services, and the culture in which they work. While TQM is concerned
with quality, the scenario describes the five phases of Six Sigma, define, measure, analyze,
improve, and control and, therefore, TQM is not the correct choice.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Six Sigma
Correct. Define, measure, analyze, improve, and control are the steps described in the
scenario for the methodology used by your organization. These are the five phases of the
Six Sigma quality improvement method.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Quality function deployment (QFD)
Incorrect. QFD is a structured method that uses seven management and planning tools,
such as affinity diagrams, relations diagrams, tree diagrams, etc., to identify and prioritize
customers’ expectations quickly and effectively. The scenario describes the five phases of
Six Sigma, define, measure, analyze, improve, and control, not the tools of QFD.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Deming's PDCA cycle
Incorrect. Deming's PDCA cycle is a four-step quality cycle consisting of plan, do, check,
and act. The scenario describes the five phases of Six Sigma, define, measure, analyze,

---

improve, and control.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 296, 275; see
also https://www.pmi.org/learning/library/six-sigma-method-applications-pm-8515

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 121 of 200
Question ID: 612793
With a product development project underway, the project manager is facilitating a risk
workshop and needs to determine the inputs for a Monte Carlo analysis. However, the costs
associated with the development of a key feature are uncertain as the feature will require the use
of new and previously untried technology.
What is the best course of action?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Develop a cumulative probability distribution
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Review the lessons learned repository
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Utilize representations of uncertainty
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Run a simulation
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What tool or technique associated with the Perform Quantitative Risk Analysis process might be
useful in determining inputs for a Monte Carlo simulation?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

As it pertains to risk management, a Monte Carlo simulation may be conducted during the
Perform Quantitative Risk Analysis process. Of the tools and techniques associated with the
Perform Quantitative Risk Analysis process, representations of uncertainty will be the most
effective in addressing the issue described by the question. A Monte Carlo Simulation is an
analysis technique where a computer model is iterated many times, with the input values chosen
at random for each iteration driven by the input data, including probability distributions and
probabilistic branches. With representations of uncertainty, the range of possible values
associated with an activity can be represented as a probability distribution. In this scenario, the
uncertain costs for developing the key feature can be represented by a probability distribution.
These values can then serve as an input to the Monte Carlo simulation. Therefore, of the

---

available options, utilizing representations of uncertainty is the best answer to the question
asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Develop a cumulative probability distribution
Incorrect. A cumulative probability distribution (S-curve) is an output from a Monte Carlo
simulation, whereas the question is asking how to determine the inputs. A probability
distribution may be an input for a Monte Carlo simulation, but not a 'cumulative'
probability distribution.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Review the lessons learned repository
Incorrect. The question indicates that the source of uncertainty is related to the use of new
and previously untried technology. As such, there is not likely to be any relevant
information regarding this technology in the lessons learned repository.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Utilize representations of uncertainty
Correct. With representations of uncertainty, the range of possible values associated with
an activity can be represented as a probability distribution. In this scenario, the uncertain
costs for developing the key feature can be represented by a probability distribution. These
values can then serve as an input to the Monte Carlo simulation.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Run a simulation
Incorrect. Simulations are typically performed using a Monte Carlo analysis. The question
states that the project manager needs to determine the inputs in order to perform this
analysis. Therefore, the project manager cannot run a simulation until the inputs are
determined.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 432
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 122 of 200
Question ID: 612607
- **A project manager has just received formal acceptance and final payment from a client for a**
software development project. The project manager needs to begin preparing the final project
report.
Which of the following will be most useful in creating the final report?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Stakeholder register
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Communications management plan
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Project charter
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Closing report register
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Where should you find high-level information about the project that would be useful in providing
a summary of project performance?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The final project report is created during the Close Project or Phase process. The final project
report provides a summary of the project performance. The project charter is an input to the
Close Project or Phase process. The project charter contains high-level information about the
project, measurable project objectives and related success criteria, and other high-level project
information which can be used to compare with actual project results to create the final project
report. Of the available options, only the project charter has information that would be relevant
in creating a summary of project performance, thus making the project charter the best answer to
the question asked.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Stakeholder register
Incorrect. Stakeholder register is a project document which includes the identification,
assessment, and classification of project stakeholders. The stakeholder register contains
useful information for creating a distribution list for the final report. However, the
stakeholder register does not have the type of high-level information that will be helpful in
preparing the final report.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Communications management plan
Incorrect. The communications management plan is a component of the project
management plan that describes how, when, and by whom information about the project
will be administered and disseminated. This information will be useful once the final report
is complete to determine how the report should be communicated. However, the
communications management plan does not contain information related to project
performance.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Project charter
Correct. The final project report provides a summary of the project performance. The
project charter will contain high-level information about the project, measurable project
objectives and related success criteria, and other high-level project information which can
be used to create the final project report.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Closing report register
Incorrect. 'Closing report register' is a fake term made up for this question.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 124, 127-128, 81
