PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 170 of 200
Question ID: 625111
Due to unforeseen challenges, it has been determined that your original budget of $500,000 is no
longer realistic. You have estimated that the project will eventually cost $600,000. The table
below represents the current status of the project. The method used to determine the earned value
is based on percent complete.
What is the cost performance efficiency that must be maintained to complete the project based
on the estimate at completion?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.1.50
BError! Not a valid embedded object.0.75
CError! Not a valid embedded object.0.88
DError! Not a valid embedded object.1.17
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**


---

The cost performance efficiency is TCPI. The formula for the TCPI based on the EAC is: TCPI =
(BAC - EV) / (EAC - AC)
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The to-complete performance index (TCPI) is a measure of the cost performance that is required
to be achieved with the remaining resources to meet a specified management goal, expressed as
the ratio of the cost to finish the outstanding work to the remaining budget. In other words, the
TCPI is the cost performance efficiency that must be maintained to complete the project based
on the specified budget. In the scenario described, the question is asking to determine the cost
performance efficiency that must be maintained to complete the project based on the estimate at
completion (EAC). In this case, the TCPI should be calculated using the formula that considers
the EAC, i.e., TCPI = (BAC - EV) / (EAC - AC), where BAC is budget at completion, EAC is
estimate at completion, EV is earned value, and AC is actual costs. The BAC for this project is
provided as $500,000 which is the planned value for the project. The EV is the sum of the
planned work completed, which, in this case, is 100% of activity 1, 100% of activity 2, and 50%
of activity 3. AC is the sum of the costs for each of the individual activities. The AC values for
each activity are provided in the chart. The EAC is given in the scenario, "You have estimated
that the project will eventually cost $600,000." Note, since the scenario mentions that the method
used to determine the earned value is based on percent complete, the earned value of a partially
completed work package is calculated by multiplying the planned value of the work package by
its the percent complete.
The calculations are as follows:
EV = EV of activity 1 + EV of activity 2 + EV of activity 3 = (1 x $15,000) + (1 x $10,000) +
(0.50 x $250,000) = $150,000
AC = AC of activity 1 + AC of activity 2 + AC of activity 3 = $14,000 + $11,000 + $175,000 =
$200,000
TCPI = (BAC - EV) / (EAC - AC) = ($500,000 - $150,000) / ($600,000 - $200,000) = 0.88
The TCPI of 0.88 means that in order to complete the project with the new budget of EAC =
$600,000 instead of the original budget of BAC = $500,000, the cost performance efficiency of
0.88 must be maintained. Note that the TCPI can also be calculated using only the BAC and not
the EAC. However, since the question indicates that the original budget is no longer valid and
provides a new estimate at completion, the EAC was used to calculate the TCPI.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

AError! Not a valid embedded object.1.50
Incorrect. This answer choice represents an incorrect usage of the TCPI formula where the
BAC and EAC are transposed.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.0.75
Incorrect. This answer choice represents the CPI, which can be calculated as: CPI = EV /
AC = $150,000 / $200,000 = 0.75. However, the question is asking for the TCPI and not
the CPI.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.0.88
Correct. The question is asking for the to-complete performance index (TCPI) based on the
estimate at completion, which can be calculated as: TCPI = (BAC - EV) / (EAC - AC) =
($500,000 - $150,000) / ($600,000 - $200,000) = 0.88.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.1.17
Incorrect. This answer choice represents the TCPI that should be maintained to complete
the project at its original budget, the BAC. The formula for such case is: TCPI = (BAC -
EV) / (BAC - AC). If the TCPI is calculated using the BAC and not including the EAC, then
the result would be 1.17. However, the question is asking for the TCPI to be calculated
using the EAC.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 266-268
Practice Standard for Earned Value Management - Second Edition, Project Management
Institute Inc., 2011, Page(s) 38-39
https://www.project-management-prepcast.com/pmp-formulas
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 171 of 200
Question ID: 612916
You are running a project to manufacture high-precision engine sub-assemblies. Your project
team is about to start internal quality testing which is planned to take at least two days. Your
sponsor calls you and informs that she will be in the neighborhood tomorrow morning. She asked
if it would be possible to inspect and sign off what you have completed so far.
What should be your response?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Rush the testing to have the deliverables verified by tomorrow
morning
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Accept the meeting request and prepare the required sign-off
form
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Tell the sponsor to expect your call as soon as deliverables are
verified
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Negotiate with the sponsor to waive quality requirements
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What is the required input for the sponsor to Validate Scope?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

According to the scenario, the team is about to start the Control Quality process to test the
deliverables and confirm the deliverables are verified. The verified deliverables are an output
from the Control Quality process and an input into the Validate Scope process where they
become accepted deliverables after the customer or sponsor accepts them. The project team must
first complete the Control Quality process in order for the sponsor to inspect and sign off on the
deliverables as part of the Validate Scope process. Therefore, of the choices provided, telling the
sponsor to expect your call as soon as deliverables are verified is the best answer to the question

---

asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Rush the testing to have the deliverables verified by
tomorrow morning
Incorrect. Rushing testing reduces the time available to take corrective action if necessary
and, therefore, may negatively affect the quality. Rushing testing just because the sponsor
happens to be in the neighborhood is unlikely to be the best course of action.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Accept the meeting request and prepare the required
sign-off form
Incorrect. This course of action does not respect the sponsor’s time, which may be wasted if
the deliverables have not been internally verified and do not meet acceptance criteria. You
should be honest about the probability that the deliverables will not yet be ready for
inspection until the originally scheduled time.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Tell the sponsor to expect your call as soon as
deliverables are verified
Correct. Telling the sponsor to expect your call as soon as deliverables are verified is in
the best interests of the project as it will give the team the time required to complete their
testing and allow for corrective and/or preventive action if the deliverables do not meet the
quality requirements.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Negotiate with the sponsor to waive quality
requirements
Incorrect. Sponsors, clients, and other stakeholder authorities certainly have the option of
waiving quality requirements. When they do so, part of the Validate Scope process is to
update the requirements documentation to reflect the waiver. Such waivers are indeed
common for discretionary dependencies. However, in machine manufacturing,
undiscovered quality issues may result in expensive scrap. If you initiate a waiver of quality
requirements just for the sake of convenience, it calls into question your commitment to
quality, making this a poor course of action.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 165, 167, 282-283, 305
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 172 of 200
Question ID: 612603
You are leading a project to build a new professional sports stadium, and you are in the process
of implementing the stakeholder engagement plan. In order to ensure continued support of the
project by the most influential stakeholders, you have arranged for a meet and greet with some of
the professional athletes that will be playing in the new stadium.
What is the best way for you to determine which stakeholders to invite to the meet and greet?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Research the lessons learned register
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Meet with the key stakeholders to determine which are the most
influential
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Read the communications management plan
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Review the stakeholder register
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Where is the best place to find stakeholder classification information which will be useful in
determining which stakeholders are the most influential and should be invited to the meet and
greet?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The question suggests that the Manage Stakeholder Engagement process is being carried out.
The stakeholder register is one of the inputs to the Manage Stakeholder Engagement process and
provides the list of project stakeholders and any information needed to execute the stakeholder
engagement plan. The stakeholder register contains stakeholder classification information which
will be useful in determining which stakeholders are the most influential and should be invited to
the meet and greet. Of the available choices, only the stakeholder register provides stakeholder
classifications, making it the best answer to the question asked.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Research the lessons learned register
Incorrect. It is not known from the question whether relevant information from earlier in
the project has been captured in the lessons learned register. Regardless, the lessons
learned register is not likely to have detailed information about stakeholder classifications
to determine which stakeholders are the most influential and should be invited to the meet
and greet.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Meet with the key stakeholders to determine which are
the most influential
Incorrect. Information about stakeholder classification is available in the stakeholder
register. Meeting with the key stakeholders to determine which are the most influential may
not result in the desired outcome. Additionally, this action is not the best use of the project
manager’s and the stakeholders’ time when the requested information is readily available
among the project documents.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Read the communications management plan
Incorrect. The communications management plan describes the methods, formats, and
technologies used for stakeholder communications. The communications management plan
will be helpful in determining the communication methods to invite the stakeholders, but it
does not provide stakeholder classification information to determine which stakeholders
are most influential and should be invited to the meet and greet.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Review the stakeholder register
Correct. The stakeholder register contains stakeholder classification information which
will be useful in determining which stakeholders are the most influential and should be
invited to the meet and greet.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 525, 514

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 173 of 200
Question ID: 612123
During project planning, a project manager allocates a dedicated team member to develop and
distribute weekly project status reports to project stakeholders.
What project document should reflect this repetitive and time-consuming task?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Project schedule
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Quality report
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Communications log
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Risk register
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Project document updates are often outputs from planning processes.
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The scenario implies that the project manager is developing the communications management
plan which is the primary output of the Plan Communications Management process. Project
document updates, such as the project schedule, are among the outputs of that process.
According to the scenario, the project manager assigns a dedicated team member to develop and
distribute the project status reports since this activity is expected to be recurring and likely time-
consuming. The project schedule presents linked activities with planned dates, duration,
milestones, and resources. This means the project schedule is the best place to document the
repetitive task of the development and distribution of the weekly project status report.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Project schedule
Correct. The project schedule is a project document that presents linked activities with
planned dates, duration, milestones, and resources. The project manager has assigned a
dedicated team member to develop and issue status reports. The project manager should
update the project schedule to reflect these communication activities.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Quality report
Incorrect. The quality report is a project document that includes quality management
issues, recommendations for corrective actions, and other information related to managing
quality on a project. This document does not describe who and when develops and
distributes weekly project status reports.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Communications log
Incorrect. The 'communications log' is a made-up term.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Risk register
Incorrect. The risk register is a repository in which the outputs of risk management
processes are recorded. The scenario does not imply that the development and distribution
of the weekly project status reports represent a risk to the project. Therefore, this repetitive
task is unlikely to be documented in the risk register.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 378

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 174 of 200
Question ID: 613662
- **A 4-week project requires that its members work side-by-side. Two developers, a designer, and a**
specialist were to work every day for the first 2 weeks. Due to limited computers, only three can
work simultaneously. You re-evaluate and see the need for developers for 4 weeks, the designer
just for the 1st half and the specialist only for 2nd half of the project.
What is the best resource optimization technique to use to re-schedule the activities to
accommodate three computers?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Crashing
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Resource smoothing
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Fast tracking
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Schedule compression
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Only one answer choice represents a resource optimization technique. This technique adjusts
activities of a schedule to fit predefined resource limits without changing the project completion
date.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

Once you re-evaluated the tasks and determined the graphic designer is only needed in weeks 1
and 2, and the e-commerce specialist is only needed in weeks 3 and 4, you discover there is
enough slack in the schedule to move the e-commerce specialist to begin work in week 3. This
change would accommodate the three-computer constraint because you would have the two
developers and the graphic designer on the three computers the first two weeks and the two
developers and the e-commerce specialist on the three computers in last two weeks. The
technique used to make these changes is called 'resource smoothing.' Resource smoothing is a
resource optimization technique that adjusts activities of a schedule to fit predefined resource

---

limits without changing the completion date. In the scenario described, resource smoothing is the
best answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Crashing
Incorrect. Crashing is a schedule compression technique used to shorten project duration
by adding additional resources. The problem in this scenario is not about duration, but
about a limited resource (i.e., computers). You can eliminate crashing just because it is a
schedule compression technique, not a resource optimization technique.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Resource smoothing
Correct. Resource smoothing is a resource optimization technique that adjusts activities of
a schedule to fit predefined resource limits without changing the completion date. The
question implies there is a free float in the project schedule. Resource smoothing often uses
float to rearrange activities. Therefore, of the choices provided, resource smoothing is the
best answer to the question asked.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Fast tracking
Incorrect. Fast tracking is a schedule compression technique where activities that were
originally planned to be done sequentially are done in parallel for at least a portion of
their duration. The scenario does not describe a situation where the schedule needs to be
adjusted to meet a deadline. The problem described is with resource utilization. Also, since
fast tracking is not a resource optimization technique, this answer choice can be
eliminated.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Schedule compression
Incorrect. Schedule compression techniques are used to shorten or accelerate the schedule
duration without reducing scope to meet project objectives. Crashing and fast tracking are
schedule compression techniques, both of which are incorrect answer choices.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 211, 215, 227
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 175 of 200
Question ID: 612442
- **A software development project is running behind schedule because the velocity of the project**
team has been slowed down by a higher than anticipated complexity of the technology used to
develop the product. To bring the project back into alignment with its objectives, the project
manager implements the planned response by fast tracking some of the testing activities.
What should the project manager do next?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Update the schedule using the project management information
system (PMIS)
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Submit a change request to update the schedule baseline to
reflect the results of fast tracking
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Submit a change request to update the issue log with the final
resolution
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Update the risk register to add the newly identified risk of higher
than anticipated complexity
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What tool or technique might be used to modify the project schedule?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The question implies that the Implement Risk Responses process is underway. Project
management information systems (PMIS) are among the tools and techniques of this process.
The PMIS can be used to update the project schedule to reflect changes resulting from fast
tracking. PMIS can include schedule, resource, and cost software to ensure that agreed-upon risk
response plans and their associated activities are integrated into the project alongside other
project activities. The incorrect answer choices represent activities which have already been
completed or are not likely to be necessary. Therefore, of the available choices, updating the

---

schedule using the project management information system (PMIS) is the next logical step for
the project manager to take in this scenario.

**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Update the schedule using the project management
information system (PMIS)
Correct. Project management information systems can include schedule, resource, and cost
software to ensure that agreed-upon risk response plans and their associated activities are
integrated into the project alongside other project activities.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Submit a change request to update the schedule baseline
to reflect the results of fast tracking
Incorrect. An approved change request is required to update the schedule baseline.
However, the question states that fast tracking is being used to bring the schedule back into
alignment with the project objectives, which suggests that the schedule baseline will not be
affected.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Submit a change request to update the issue log with the
final resolution
Incorrect. The question does not state whether or not the issue was captured in the issue
log. Assuming the issue was recorded in the issue log, it should be updated with the final
resolution. However, an approved change request is not likely to be required to update the
issue log. The project baselines and project management plan are typically placed in
configuration control as defined by the configuration management plan. The issue log is a
project document which is not likely to be placed under configuration control. Unless
stated otherwise, it can be assumed that the issue log is not a controlled document and,
therefore, does not require an approved change request to be modified.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Update the risk register to add the newly identified risk
of higher than anticipated complexity
Incorrect. The question states that the project manager is implementing the agreed-upon
response plan by fast tracking some of the product testing activities. A risk response plan
cannot be implemented if the risk for which the response was planned was not previously
identified. Therefore, the risk of higher than anticipated complexity must have already been
identified earlier in the project.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**

---

Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 451

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 176 of 200
Question ID: 625215
You were hired to lead external implementation projects as well as internal operations projects.
Knowing that the distinction between projects and operations is critical, you stress that difference
to project staff and stakeholders in your first project meeting. You are asked by a stakeholder if
there are any situations that operations and projects will intersect.
How should you respond to the stakeholder's question?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Operations and projects never intersect.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Operations and projects may intersect only at the closeout of the
project.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Operations and projects always intersect.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Operations and projects may intersect at each closeout phase.
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Consider that there may be several iterations within a project that might require interaction
between operations and projects.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The PMBOK® Guide discusses the differences between projects and operations, defining
operations as ongoing and a project as temporary. It also discusses the relationship between the
two areas and its importance. The guide then lists several examples of when operations and
projects may intersect. One example includes closeout phases.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Operations and projects never intersect.
Incorrect. The PMBOK® Guide discusses the differences between projects and operations,
defining operations as ongoing and a project as temporary. Saying that operations and
projects 'never' intersect would be inaccurate. The guide then lists several examples of
when operations and projects may intersect. Beware of absolute statements such as, 'never',
'always', etc.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Operations and projects may intersect only at the
closeout of the project.
Incorrect. It is true that the closeout of the project can be one of the various points that
operations and projects intersect. However, saying that this happens 'only' at the closeout
would be inaccurate. The guide suggests that each closeout phase can be an intersect point,
not 'only' the close of the entire project.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Operations and projects always intersect.
Incorrect. The PMBOK® Guide discusses the differences between projects and operations,
defining operations as ongoing and a project as temporary. The guide then lists several
examples of when operations and projects may intersect. But it does not mean they 'always'
intersect. Beware of absolute statements such as, 'never', 'always', etc.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Operations and projects may intersect at each closeout
phase.
Correct. The guide suggests that each closeout phase can be a point that operations and
projects intersect which makes this choice the best answer to the question asked.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 16

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 177 of 200
Question ID: 613222
- **A project manager is about to close a project that missed its performance goals. The project**
manager is gathering the information that is most pertinent to the project’s poor performance.
Which of the following is least likely to help in this task?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Risk report
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Project team assignments
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Assumption log
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Change log
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which answer choice is not typically used as an input into the Close Project or Phase process.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

Project team assignments document the team members and their roles and responsibilities for the
project. Documentation can include a project team directory and names inserted into the project
management plan, such as the project organization charts and schedules. Project team
assignments are not typically used as an input into the Close Project or Phase process. Although
there may be circumstances where the project team assignments might be helpful, it is the least
likely to be used compared to the other choices. The risk report, assumption log, and change log
are likely to have valuable information on aspects of the project that were problematic. Since the
question is asking for the item that would be 'least' likely to be used for the closing process,
project team assignments represent the best response.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Risk report
Incorrect. The risk report provides information on the risk status and is used to check that
there are no open risks at the end of the project. The risk report might provide insight into
any false perceptions of overall project risk.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Project team assignments
Correct. Project team assignments are not typically used as inputs to the Close Project or
Phase process, and although there might be cases where it could help, it is least likely
compared to the other choices.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Assumption log
Incorrect. The assumption log has a record of all the assumptions and constraints that
guided the technical specifications, estimates, schedule, risks, etc. For example, the
assumption log might provide valuable information on assumptions that were proved to be
false.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Change log
Incorrect. The change log contains the status of all change requests throughout the project.
The change log may provide insight into how changes negatively affected the project.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 124

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 178 of 200
Question ID: 612017
To mitigate recent labor issues and reduce their risk in the future, senior executives are
considering alternatives for automating production. One executive is not in favor of using
automation at all; a second executive suggests adding some basic automation, while another is in
favor of automating the entire production line.
Which of the following is the least likely option to be included in the business case?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Do nothing
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Do less than the minimum work possible to address the problem
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Do more than the minimum work possible to address the problem
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Do the minimum work possible to address the problem
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which option makes the least sense from a business perspective?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

- **A business case should include a set of options to be considered for addressing the business**
problem or opportunity. Options are alternative courses of action that may be taken by the
organization. Doing less than the minimum work possible to address the problem makes the least
sense from a business perspective. Taking this option means that the company would expend
company resources without receiving the benefits of the project. Why would the company
authorize a project that does not produce the intended benefits?

**Details for Each Option:**


---

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Do nothing
Incorrect. Selecting this option results in the project not being authorized. This option is
also referred to as the "business as usual" option. Declining to authorize a desired or
optional project is always a possibility.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Do less than the minimum work possible to address the
problem
Correct. Doing less than the minimum work possible to address the problem makes the
least sense from a business perspective. Taking this option means that the company would
expend company resources without receiving the benefits of the project. Why would the
company authorize a project that does not produce the intended benefits?
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Do more than the minimum work possible to address the
problem
Incorrect. This option meets the minimum set of criteria and some or all of the other
documented criteria. For example, in the scenario, perhaps the company would authorize
the project to replace the entire production line with a new automated system rather than
just retrofit the existing production line.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Do the minimum work possible to address the problem
Incorrect. The minimum work possible meets the minimum set of criteria for the project.
For this scenario, that might mean retrofitting the existing production line to incorporate
automation.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 31

Question 179 of 200
Question ID: 612409
- **A project manager has completed the project management plan which has just been reviewed and**
approved by the project sponsor and others. The project manager now needs to communicate the
start of the project along with key milestones, and other relevant information to inform the
stakeholders and gain commitment.
What is the best way to accomplish these objectives?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Provide copies of the project management plan
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Email the milestone schedule
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Share the project charter on the company internal website
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Conduct a meeting
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Review of the planning domain of the Project Management Professional (PMP)® Examination
Content Outline will be helpful in correctly answering this question.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The Project Management Professional (PMP)® Examination Content Outline contains a list of
tasks for each domain, with which PMP aspirants are expected to be familiar. Task #12 of the
planning domain of the Project Management Professional (PMP)® Examination Content Outline
states, "Conduct kick-off meeting, communicating the start of the project, key milestones, and
other relevant information in order to inform and engage stakeholders and gain commitment."
Therefore, of the choices given, conducting a meeting is the best answer to the question asked.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Provide copies of the project management plan
Incorrect. Providing the project management plan suggests one-way communication.
Interactive communication is a more effective method of gaining the commitment of key
stakeholders as it will allow the stakeholders to ask questions and have their concerns
addressed.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Email the milestone schedule
Incorrect. A milestone schedule is a type of schedule that presents milestones with planned
dates. While the milestone schedule will have key milestones, it does not contain other
relevant information nor is it the appropriate method of communicating the start of a
project or gaining commitment from the stakeholders.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Share the project charter on the company internal
website
Incorrect. The project charter contains some high-level information regarding the project.
However, sharing the project charter does not allow for interaction with the stakeholders,
and is therefore not the best way to gain commitment from the stakeholders, making this an
incorrect response.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Conduct a meeting
Correct. Task #12 of the planning domain of the Project Management Professional
(PMP)® Examination Content Outline states, "Conduct kick-off meeting, communicating
the start of the project, key milestones, and other relevant information in order to inform
and engage stakeholders and gain commitment." Conducting a kick-off meeting would be a
better answer; however, this choice is not provided. Therefore, of the available options,
conducting a meeting, implying the kick-off meeting, is the best answer.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 86; see also Project Management Professional
(PMP)® Examination Content Outline, Project Management Institute Inc., June 2015, Domain 2,
Task 12

- **A key project deliverable has been outsourced to a vendor. The vendor delivered on contract, and**

process.
What should the project manager do next?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Pay the vendor's invoice
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Approve the deliverable received from the vendor
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Conduct an audit
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Measure stakeholder satisfaction

After procurements are closed, the process of administrative closure of the project should begin.
What activity is part of this process?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

According to the scenario, the Control Procurements process has already been completed. Three
of the four answer choices represent activities, which are typically performed during the Control
Procurements process and, therefore, can be eliminated. Measuring stakeholder satisfaction is
part of the Close Project or Phase process. Therefore, of the choices provided, after completing
the activities associated with the Control Procurements process, measuring stakeholder
satisfaction is what the project manager should do next.

---

phase includes measuring stakeholder satisfaction. Stakeholders' feedback can lead to
improved processes and procedures for future projects. Of the available choices, only

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 181 of 200
Question ID: 613601
- **A construction company which is very experienced with building apartments has been contracted**
to build a strip mall which is a relatively new type of project for the organization. The project is
now concluded, and the project team has documented a significant amount of new knowledge
gained throughout the project.
Where would a project manager find this information when planning their future similar project?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Lessons learned repository
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Project knowledge register
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Lessons learned register
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Project management body of knowledge
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Where is knowledge gained during a project transferred at the end of a project?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The lessons learned register is an output of the Manage Project Knowledge process. It is then
used as an input and updated as an output in many processes throughout the project. The
knowledge gained throughout the project can then be used to improve performance for the
current project. At the end of the project or phase, the information is transferred to an
organizational process asset called a lessons learned repository for use in future projects. A
future project manager working on a subsequent project can access the knowledge gained on past
projects from the lessons learned repository.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Lessons learned repository
Correct. Lessons learned and knowledge gained throughout a project are transferred to the
lessons learned repository at the end of a project or phase for use in future projects.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Project knowledge register
Incorrect. 'Project knowledge register' is a fake term made up for this question.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Lessons learned register
Incorrect. Lessons learned register is a project document used to record knowledge gained
during a project so that it can be used in the current project. At the end of the project or
phase, the information is transferred to an organizational process asset called a lessons
learned repository for use in future projects.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Project management body of knowledge
Incorrect. Project management body of knowledge is a term that describes the knowledge
within the profession of project management. It has nothing to do with the repository of
knowledge gained throughout project execution.

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 104, 128

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 182 of 200
Question ID: 612261
You have been hired midway into project execution to replace the previous project manager. The
project is in disarray: discussions on changes frequently become shouting matches between the
project team members, no one seems to take responsibility, and the project management plan is
incomplete. As a result, the project is far behind schedule.
What is your best course of action?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Use management reserves to cover for the lost time
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Seek help from the project management office (PMO)
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Fire the project team members and outsource the work
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Revise the project management plan and have it approved
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What is the most likely reason for the changes to trigger such heated discussions?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The scenario describes a project in execution after the initial project manager leaves. Since the
project management plan is incomplete, and discussions on changes to deliverables frequently
become shouting matches between the project team members, it is reasonable to assume that the
change management plan is the main cause of the flawed or even missing change control process
on the project. Reviewing the project management plan, specifically the change management
plan, and making necessary modifications to ensure changes are properly managed on the project
from now on is essential for the project to proceed.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Use management reserves to cover for the lost time
Incorrect. Management reserves are part of the overall project budget allocated to cover
the unforeseen risks that can affect a project. While the situation described in the scenario
can be considered an unforeseen risk, using management reserves without addressing the
root cause of the problem is unlikely to be your best course of action.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Seek help from the project management office (PMO)
Incorrect. The PMO is an organizational structure that standardizes the project-related
governance processes and facilitates the sharing of resources, methodologies, tools, and
techniques. Depending on its type (supportive, controlling, directive), the PMO may
provide guidance and help you in the situation described in the scenario. However, another
choice represents a better answer to the question.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Fire the project team members and outsource the work
Incorrect. There is not enough information in the question to determine that the team is the
source of the problems the project has been experiencing so far. Therefore, without proper
investigation, firing the team would be an overreaction.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Revise the project management plan and have it
approved
Correct. To manage the project, it is vital for you, as a project manager, to have a complete
and approved project management plan.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 116

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 183 of 200
Question ID: 613615
- **A project manager is leading a project and is currently preparing the project planning documents.**
In support of this process, the project manager must gather information to determine how work
will be executed to accomplish the project objectives.
What is the best way for the project manager to perform this task?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Review the project charter
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Schedule a bidder conference
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Schedule a meeting with the appropriate stakeholders
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Consult the project management plan
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What is the best way for the project manager to gather information from key stakeholders?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The question implies the project manager is conducting the Develop Project Management Plan
process. One of the tools and techniques associated with the Develop Project Management Plan
process is the use of meetings. Meetings may be used to discuss the project approach, determine
how work will be executed to accomplish the project objectives and establish the way the project
will be monitored and controlled. Of the answer choices provided, gathering the appropriate
stakeholders together for a meeting is the best way for the project manager to perform the task at
hand.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Review the project charter
Incorrect. The project charter contains high-level information about the project but does
not provide the level of detail required to determine how the work will be executed.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Schedule a bidder conference
Incorrect. Bidder conferences are used during the Conduct Procurements process as
opposed to the Develop Project Management Plan which, based on the information
provided in the question, is the process the project manager is performing.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Schedule a meeting with the appropriate stakeholders
Correct. The question implies the project manager is conducting the Develop Project
Management Plan process. For this process, meetings are used to discuss the project
approach, determine how work will be executed to accomplish the project objectives and
establish the way the project will be monitored and controlled.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Consult the project management plan
Incorrect. The question implies that the Develop Project Management Plan process is
underway, suggesting that the project management plan is not ready yet and, therefore,
cannot be used as a resource.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 86

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 184 of 200
Question ID: 612353
You are developing the project management plan for your current project. You want to know if
there is any relevant information from past projects that can help you with your task.
What should you do?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Review the lessons learned register
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Research the organizational process assets
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Meet with a project manager who managed similar past projects
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Check the enterprise environmental factors for lessons learned
from past projects
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Where might you find lessons learned from past projects?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The question is asking where to find information on lessons learned from past projects. The
lessons learned repository is an organizational process asset which serves as a store of historical
information about lessons learned from past projects. Therefore, researching the organizational
process assets is the best answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Review the lessons learned register
Incorrect. The lessons learned register is a source for information on the ‘current’ project,

---

while the question states that you want to know if there is any relevant information from
‘past’ projects. Information on past projects is contained in the lessons learned repository
rather than the lessons learned register.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Research the organizational process assets
Correct. The lessons learned repository is an organizational process asset which serves as
a store of historical information about lessons learned from past projects. Therefore,
researching the organizational process assets is the best answer to the question asked.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Meet with a project manager who managed similar past
projects
Incorrect. While the project manager of similar past projects may have some relevant
information, this information reflects only one opinion. Checking the organizational
process assets is a better answer choice because the lessons learned repository is more
likely to have complete and accurate information reflecting the views of all project team
members. Therefore, this answer choice can be eliminated.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Check the enterprise environmental factors for lessons
learned from past projects
Incorrect. The lessons learned repository is an organizational process asset and not an
enterprise environmental factor. The enterprise environmental factors are not a source of
information on past projects, making this choice an incorrect response.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 84

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 185 of 200
Question ID: 613226
- **A project is completing late and over budget. There were no major issues, quality problems, or**
changes, and only a few of the risks needed response actions. The project manager is trying to
determine what has caused the problem.
Which of the following is most likely to point to the root cause?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Milestone list
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Change log
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Basis of estimates
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Quality reports
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The root cause of the problem most likely occurred in an early part of the project.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The basis of estimates contains supporting documentation outlining the details used in
establishing project estimates such as assumptions, constraints, level of detail, ranges, and
confidence levels. The basis of estimates is used as an input to the Close Project or Phase process
implied by the scenario to evaluate how the estimation of durations, cost, resources, and cost
control compared to the actual results. Sometimes, selecting the correct answer requires the
prospective PMP aspirants to use the process of elimination of the worst answer choices.
According to the scenario, the project did not encounter any major issues, quality problems, or
changes, and only a few risks have realized necessitating the implementation of the response
plans. This information may help eliminate the answer choices related to the scope, schedule,
cost, quality, risks, etc., leaving the basis of estimates as not ideal but the only plausible answer
choice.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Milestone list
Incorrect. The milestone list indicates might indicate 'when' key milestones were missed but
would not likely indicate 'why' they were missed.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Change log
Incorrect. The change log contains a comprehensive list of changes submitted during the
project and their current status. The question states that there were no major changes to
the project. Additionally, if scope creep occurred, the change log would not be helpful,
since scope creep is uncontrolled and if the change were logged, the change would have
likely been controlled.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Basis of estimates
Correct. Since the project did not encounter any major issues and the few realized risks
were addressed with response plans, it is likely that the cost and schedule estimates were
flawed. The basis of estimates may be helpful in identifying the issues with the estimates.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Quality reports
Incorrect. The question states that there were no major quality issues encountered during
the project. Therefore, the quality reports are not likely to provide useful information to
identify the reason the project failed to meet its objectives.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 124

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 186 of 200
Question ID: 625211
One of your project team members, who was responsible for several key deliverables, has
suddenly left the company. You overhear a heated debate among the team members over what to
do next. It sounds as if the team is split - half want to hire a new team member; the other half
want to contract out the work. As the project manager, you want to resolve this conflict in a way
that solves the problem and keeps the team unified.
Which of the following approaches should you take?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Tell the team that you are in charge and will take disciplinary
action if a consensus is not reached
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Agree with the team that a resource is needed, and urge one side
to back down for the sake of agreement
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Ask the team members to find a compromise that would be
acceptable to both sides
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Request that the team researches different options, presents
ideas, and works out a solution
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which conflict management approach is considered a win-win conflict resolution technique?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

PMI prefers problem solving and collaboration when it comes to resolving issues or conflicts, as
it is a win-win conflict resolution technique that typically leads to greater buy-in and the most
lasting solution. The 'collaborate/problem solve' approach emphasizes open dialogue,
cooperation, and incorporating multiple viewpoints to find the best outcome for the project. In
this scenario, the project manager sends the project team on a fact-finding mission, which is a
good way to help the team discuss the issue more objectively. Getting the team together in a

---

problem-solving session to present their ideas and work out a solution is more likely to satisfy
both sides and keep the team unified; therefore, the 'Collaborate/Problem Solve' approach is the
'best' answer choice. All other approaches are temporary solutions resulting in recurring
conflicts.

**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Tell the team that you are in charge and will take
disciplinary action if a consensus is not reached
Incorrect. This is an example of the 'Force/Direct' approach to resolving a conflict.
Forcing a solution on the team is a win-lose scenario and will likely divide the team rather
than unite it. Disciplinary actions are not warranted at this stage since project team
members are entitled to have differences of opinion, which when managed properly can
result in greater productivity and positive working relationships. If project team members
cannot resolve a conflict situation on their own, a project manager should help facilitate a
satisfactory resolution before taking disciplinary action.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Agree with the team that a resource is needed, and urge
one side to back down for the sake of agreement
Incorrect. This is an example of the 'Smooth/Accommodate' approach to conflict resolution.
Emphasizing areas of agreement between warring sides can help diffuse conflict situations
but leave the real issue buried. Urging one side to back down simply to maintain the peace
puts maintaining harmony within the group above finding the best solution to the problem.
This approach is not very satisfying and could lead to breakdowns in trust.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Ask the team members to find a compromise that would
be acceptable to both sides
Incorrect. This sounds like a nice answer, but 'Compromise/Reconcile' is a lose-lose
conflict resolution technique because each side has to give up something to reach a
solution, meaning that no one gets what they wanted. This only partially or temporarily
resolves the conflict and therefore is not the best choice.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Request that the team researches different options,
presents ideas, and works out a solution
Correct. This 'Collaborate/Problem Solve' approach allows the team to gather facts to help
them make an objective decision and work collaboratively to work out a solution.
Collaboration and problem solving are the best ways to resolve conflict as they are likely to
produce a win-win result.

---


**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 349
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results
Prev Next

Question 187 of 200
Question ID: 613612
As the project manager, you are in the process of assisting the project sponsor with creating the
project charter for a project which will design and launch a new social media platform. In order
to create the project charter, you need to get a better understanding of the project's objectives.
What should you do to obtain this information?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Consult the project management plan
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Review the assumption log
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Check the project needs analysis documents
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Review the business case and benefits management plan
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which documents serve as an input to the Develop Project Charter process and are sources of
information about the project's objectives and how the project will contribute to the business
goals?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The question suggests that the Develop Project Charter process is underway. Business
documents including the business case and the benefits management plan serve as an input to the
Develop Project Charter process. These business documents are sources of information about the
project's objectives and how the project will contribute to the business goals. Therefore, to get a
better understanding of the project's objectives, you should review the business case and benefits
management plan.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Consult the project management plan
Incorrect. The question implies that the Develop Project Charter process is being carried
out. The project management plan is created after the project charter is developed.
Therefore, the project management plan is not available at that point nor does it contain
information about the project's objectives.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Review the assumption log
Incorrect. The assumption log contains assumptions and constraints identified throughout
the project life cycle. This document does not contain information about the project's
objectives.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Check the project needs analysis documents
Incorrect. 'Project needs analysis documents' is a fake term made up for this question.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Review the business case and benefits management plan
Correct. Business documents including the business case and the benefits management plan
are sources of information about the project's objectives and how the project will
contribute to the business goals.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 77; see also https://www.pmi.org/-
/media/pmi/documents/public/pdf/learning/thought-leadership/benefits-realization-management-
framework.pdf

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 188 of 200
Question ID: 610065
- **A project manager is in the process of developing the stakeholder register. As the first step in this**
process, she needs to create a list of potential stakeholders and decides to use a data gathering
technique called brain writing.
What is the first thing to do when using that technique?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Convene a data gathering meeting with the participants
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Develop your own template for a stakeholder register
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Send a list of questions to participants before the creativity
session
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Consult the stakeholder management plan to understand how the
stakeholders are to be identified
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What differentiates brain writing from a traditional brainstorming session?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

Data gathering techniques that can be used for the Identify Stakeholders process include
questionnaires and surveys, brainstorming, and brain writing. Brain writing is a refinement of
brainstorming that allows individual participants time to consider the questions individually
before the group creativity session is held. Therefore, the first step of brain writing is providing
the participants with the questions before the creativity session. This process will allow the
participants to be better prepared which will make the meeting more effective than a traditional
brainstorming session.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Convene a data gathering meeting with the participants
Incorrect. Brain writing is a data gathering technique where participants are allowed time
to consider the questions individually before the brainstorming session. Therefore, the
project manager needs to provide the participants with the questions before convening the
data gathering meeting.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Develop your own template for a stakeholder register
Incorrect. The project manager would need a template for the stakeholder register upon
starting the process of identifying stakeholders. However, she is not likely to develop her
own template. The project manager should first check the organizational process assets for
an approved version of the stakeholder register template. Therefore, this answer choice can
be eliminated.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Send a list of questions to participants before the
creativity session
Correct. Brain writing is a refinement of brainstorming that allows individual participants
time to consider the questions individually before the group creativity session is held.
Therefore, the first step of brain writing is providing the participants with the questions
before the creativity session.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Consult the stakeholder management plan to understand
how the stakeholders are to be identified
Incorrect. The question states that the project manager is in the process of creating the
stakeholder register. The stakeholder register is developed during the first iteration of the
Identify Stakeholders process. Therefore, the stakeholder management plan, as a
component of the project management plan, does not yet exist, making this option an
incorrect response.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 511

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 189 of 200
Question ID: 612498
- **A project manager is leading a project to develop a prototype diesel engine. One problem that**
was identified and documented was the corrosion of engine parts which were stored in an offsite
storage facility. The parts were refinished and coated with a penetrant to inhibit corrosion in the
future. The project manager is confident that these measures will solve the problem.
With respect to tools and techniques, what else should the project manager do in this situation?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Perform an alternative analysis
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Update the lessons learned register
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Revise the issue log
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Determine if the problem has been resolved
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What else should be done in this scenario with respect to problem solving?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The question describes a situation where a problem occurred on the project, and measures were
taken to resolve the issue suggesting that problem solving was used in this case. Problem solving
may use a set of tools that helps the project manager to solve problems that arise during Control
Resources, the process implied by the scenario. Although the question states that the project
manager is confident that the steps taken will solve the problem, there is no way to determine the
effectiveness of the solution at this point. The solution should be checked to ensure that the
problem has been indeed fixed. In this case, that might involve periodically inspecting the parts
and reapplying the penetrant as necessary. The final step of the problem solving process is to
check the solution which is all that remains to be completed in this scenario with respect to tools
and techniques. The incorrect answer choices represent actions that do not involve tools and

---

techniques or have already been completed.

**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Perform an alternative analysis
Incorrect. An alternative analysis is a technique used to evaluate identified options in order
to select the options or approaches to use to execute and perform the work of the project.
Although not stated in the question, it is reasonable to assume that an alternative analysis
may have been performed to decide between repairing or replacing the damaged parts. The
question states that the affected parts were refinished indicating that the decision has
already been made and corrective actions were taken. Therefore, even if the alternative
analysis was not performed in this scenario, performing it now has little value since the
action to address the issue has already been taken.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Update the lessons learned register
Incorrect. The lessons learned register is a project document used to record knowledge
gained during a project so that it can be used in the current project and entered into the
lessons learned repository. Although the lessons learned register should be updated in this
situation, the question is asking about tools and techniques, whereas the lessons learned
register is a project document, making this choice an incorrect answer.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Revise the issue log
Incorrect. The issue log is a project document where information about issues is recorded
and monitored. While the issue log should be updated with the details regarding this
problem, the issue log is a project document and not a tool or technique as asked by the
question.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Determine if the problem has been resolved
Correct. Although the question states that the project manager is confident that the steps
taken will solve the problem, there is no way to determine the effectiveness of the solution
at this point. As the final step in the problem solving process, the solution should be
checked to ensure that the problem has been fixed.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 356, 358

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 190 of 200
Question ID: 612642
- **A project manager is leading a project which has experienced numerous quality issues. These**
issues threaten the successful completion of the project objectives. In order to improve the
performance of the project, the project manager schedules a retrospective with the project team
and relevant stakeholders.
Which of the following topics is least likely to be discussed?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.What to incorporate into the ongoing project and what to include
in future projects
BError! Not a valid embedded object.What are the project objectives and the roles and responsibilities
of the stakeholders
CError! Not a valid embedded object.What elements of the project have gone well and what could be
improved upon
DError! Not a valid embedded object.What should be added to the organizational process assets (OPAs)
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which answer choice represents a topic more appropriately discussed during the project kick-off
meeting?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The question suggests that the Control Quality is being performed, and a retrospective, among
the tools and techniques used in this process, is being held to determine how to address the
quality issues that have been encountered during the project. A retrospective is a scheduled
review to record lessons learned which can then be documented in the lessons learned register to
improve the future performance of the project. Appropriate topics of discussion for the
retrospective would be successful elements of the project, what could be improved, what to
incorporate in the ongoing project and what to include in future projects, and what to add to the

---

organizational process assets.
The purpose of a project kick-off meeting is to communicate the objectives of the project, gain
the commitment of the team for the project, and explain the roles and responsibilities of each
stakeholder. Note, the question is asking which answer choice represents a topic that is 'least'
likely to be discussed. Therefore, of the available choices, the objectives of the project and the
roles and responsibilities of each stakeholder are 'least' likely to be discussed in this scenario.

**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.What to incorporate into the ongoing project and what to
include in future projects
Incorrect. During the retrospective, many suggestions may be made to address the quality
issues faced during the project. Some of the suggestions may not be relevant or actionable.
- **A discussion of what to incorporate into the project will be vital to addressing the quality**
issues.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.What are the project objectives and the roles and
responsibilities of the stakeholders
Correct. The purpose of a project kick-off meeting is to communicate the objectives of the
project, gain the commitment of the team for the project, and explain the roles and
responsibilities of each stakeholder. This answer choice best represents the project kick-off
meeting rather than a retrospective and is, therefore, the best answer to the question asked.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.What elements of the project have gone well and what
could be improved upon
Incorrect. The project team will want to discuss what has gone well thus far on the project
and what could be improved upon to address the quality issues for the project. This
information will be a source of best practices which can be documented in the lessons
learned register for use later in the project. Identifying the problem areas can lead to a
productive discussion about what specific actions can be taken to improve quality for the
project going forward.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.What should be added to the organizational process
assets (OPAs)
Incorrect. OPAs are the plans, processes, policies, procedures, and knowledge bases
specific to and used by the performing organization. While updates to the OPAs are not
explicitly specified as an output from the Control Quality process implied by the question,
the retrospective meeting can result in suggestions of how the OPAs should be updated.

---


**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 86, 305

PMP Exam 4
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 191 of 200
Question ID: 612502
- **A vendor on your project informs you that they will be unable to perform the work as contracted**
after some equipment required for the project was destroyed in a hurricane. The vendor cites a
clause in the contract that is designed to address the inability of a party to execute their
responsibilities due to extraordinary factors that were outside the control of the party?
What clause does the vendor refer to?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Arbitration
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Force majeure
CError! Not a valid embedded object.No-contest
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Termination
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The correct answer is also referred to as an act of God clause.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

- **A force majeure clause is a common contractual clause that frees parties, bound by a contract,**
from liability or obligation when certain circumstances beyond their control arise making
performance impossible. Examples of force majeure may include war, riot, strikes, flooding,
tornado, hurricanes, etc. The scenario describes a hurricane as destroying the equipment needed
to execute the project, which is an example of a force majeure. While the topic of this question is
not included in the PMBOK® Guide, the Project Management Professional (PMP)® Examination
Content Outline, June 2015, covers knowledge and skills, such as contract management
techniques, with which PMP aspirants are expected to be familiar. The force majeure clause is
one of these topics.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Arbitration
Incorrect. An arbitration clause requires that the parties resolve any disputes through an
arbitration process as opposed to using the courts. However, in the event of a natural
disaster, a party to a contract cannot use an arbitration clause to seek relief from
contractual obligations.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Force majeure
Correct. A force majeure clause is a common contractual clause that frees parties, bound
by a contract, from liability or obligation when certain circumstances beyond their control
arise making performance impossible. Examples of force majeure include war, riot, strikes,
flooding, tornado, hurricanes, etc.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.No-contest
Incorrect. A no-contest clause is designed to threaten another party with litigation or
criminal prosecution if they fail to take action or to cease a certain action. The no-contest
clause is not applicable in the event of a natural disaster.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Termination
Incorrect. The termination clause offers a release of the contractual obligation of a party in
the event that the other party to the contract breaches the agreement. The question
describes a natural disaster which renders a party to the contract unable to fulfill their
obligation rather than a breach of the contract.

**Reference:**

https://www.projectmanagement.com/blog-post/8555/How-Project-Managers-Can-Execute-
Force-Majeure-Clauses; see also https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Category:Contract_clauses
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

Question ID: 612455
The project team is just starting the process of developing approaches to involve project

support of this process, the project manager is advising the team to review information regarding
the project purpose, objectives, and success criteria.
What is the best way for the team to obtain this information?
AError! Not a valid embedded object.Ask the project sponsor
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Study the stakeholder engagement plan
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Examine the stakeholder engagement assessment matrix
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Review the project charter

What project document is available during project planning that contains high-level information
on the project?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The question suggests that the team is starting the Plan Stakeholder Engagement process. The
project charter is one of the inputs into this process. The project charter contains information on
the project purpose, objectives, and success criteria. Therefore, reviewing the project charter is
the most appropriate action for the project team to take in this scenario.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

AError! Not a valid embedded object.Ask the project sponsor

sponsor. Therefore, this is not the best answer choice.
BError! Not a valid embedded object.Study the stakeholder engagement plan

stakeholder engagement plan is not yet available to be used as a resource.
CError! Not a valid embedded object.Examine the stakeholder engagement assessment matrix
Incorrect. The question suggests that the Plan Stakeholder Engagement process is being
performed, and a stakeholder engagement assessment matrix is a data representation
technique that may be used during this process. Since the Plan Stakeholder Engagement
process is just getting started, the stakeholder engagement assessment matrix has yet to be
created. Additionally, the stakeholder engagement assessment matrix does not contain the
information requested.
DError! Not a valid embedded object.Review the project charter
Correct. The project charter contains information on the project purpose, objectives, and
success criteria. Therefore, reviewing the project charter is the most appropriate action for
